%       \begin{multicols}{5} 
%ṭranlsliteration credits: ajarve@fms30/cca/rockvell/com (āhto Jarve)
\medskip\hrule\medskip

         atha pratyantardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ || 61||

\medskip

pṛthak svasvadaśāmānairhanyādantardaśāmitim |
bhyetsarvadaśāyogaiḥ phalaṃ pratyantaraṃ kramāt || 1||

vivādo vittahāniśca dārārtiḥ śirasi vyathā |
ravyantare budhairjñeyaṃ tasya pratyantare phalam || 2||

udvegaḥ kalahaścaiva vittahānirmanovyathā |
ravyantare vijānīyāt candrapratyantare phalam || 3||

rājabhītiḥ śastrabhītirbandhanaṃ bahusaṃkaṭam |
sa/truvahnikṛtā pīḍā kujapratyantare phalam || 4||

śleṣmavyādhiḥ śastrabhītiedhanahānirmahadbhayam |
rājabhaṅgastathā trāso rāhupratyantare phalam || 5||

śatrunāśo jayo vṛddhirvastrahemādibhūṣaṇam |
aśvayānādilābhaśca gurupratyantare phalam || 6||

dhanahāniḥ paśoḥ pīḍā mahodvego mahārujaḥ |
aśubhaṃ sarvamāpnoti śanipratyantare janaḥ || 7||

vidyālābho bandhusaṅga bhojyaprāptirdhanāgamaḥ |
dharmalābho nṛpātpūjā bidhapratyantare bhavet || 8||

prāṇabhītirmahāhānī rājabhītiśca vigrahaḥ |
śatruṇāñca mahāvādo ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 9||

dināni samarūpāṇi lābho'pyalpo bhavediha |
svalpā ca sukhasampattiḥ śukrapratyantare bhavet || 10||

bhūmojyadhanasamprāptī rājapūjāmahatsukham |
lābhaścandrāntare jñeyaṃ candrapratyantare phalam || 11||

mativṛddhirmahāpūjyaḥ sukhaṃ bandhujanaiḥ saha |
dhanāgamaḥ śatrubhayaṃ kujapratyantare bhavet || 12||

bhavetkalyāṇasampattī rājavittasamāgamaḥ |
aśubhairalpamṛtyuaśca rāhupratyantare dvija || 13||

vastralābho mahātejo brahmajñānaṃ ca sadguroḥ |
rājyālaṃkaraṇāvāptirgurupratyantare phalam || 14||

durdine labhate pīḍāṃ vātapittādviśeṣataḥ |
dhanadhānyayaśohāniḥ śanipratyantare bhavet || 15||

putrajanmahayaprāptirvidyālābho mahonnatiḥ |
śuklavastrānnalābhaśca budhapratyantare bhavet || 16||

brāhmaṇena samaṃ yuddhamapamṛtyuḥ sukhakṣayaḥ |
sarvatra jāyate kleśaḥ ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 17||

dhanalābho mahatsaukhyaṃ kanyājanma subhojanam |
prītiśca sarvalokebhyo bhṛgupratyantare vidhoḥ || 18||

annāgamo vastralābhaḥ śatruhāniḥ sukhāgamaḥ |
sarvatra vijayaprāptiḥ sūryapratyantare vidhoḥ || 19||

śatrubhītiṃ kaliṃ ghoraṃ raktasrāvaṃ mṛterbhayam |
kujasyāntardaśāyāṃ ca kujapratyantare vadet || 20||

bandhanaṃ rājabhaṅgaśca dhanahāniḥ kubhojanam |
kalahaḥ śatrubhirnityaṃ rāhupratyantare bhavet || 21||

matināśastathā duḥkhaṃ santāpaḥ kalaho bhavet |
viphalaṃ cintitaṃ sarvaṃ guroḥ pratyantare bhavet || 22||

svāmināśastathā pīḍā dhanahānirnmahābhayam |
vaikalyaṃ kalahastrāso śaneḥ pratyantare bhavet || 23||

sarvathā buddhināśaśca dhanahānirjvarastanau |
vastrānnasuhṛdāṃ nāśo budhapratyantare bhavet || 24||

ālasya ca śiraḥpīḍā pāparogo'pamṛtyukṛt |
rājabhītiḥ śastraghāto ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 25||

cāṇḍālātsaṅkaṭastrāso rājaśāstrabhayaṃ bhavet |
atisārā'tha vamanaṃ bhṛgoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 26||

bhūmilābho'rthasampattiḥ santoṣo mitrasaṅgatiḥ |
sarvatra sukhamāpnoti raveḥ pratyantare janaḥ || 27||

yāmyāṃ diśi bhavellābhaḥ sitavastravibhūṣaṇam |
saṃsiddhiḥ sarvakāryāṇāṃ vidhoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 28||

bandhanaṃ bahudhā rogo bahughātaḥ suhṛdbhayam |
rāhvantardaśāyāṃ ca jñeyaṃ rāhvantare phalam || 29||

sarvatra labhate mānaṃ gajāśvaṃ ca dhanāgamam |
rāhorantardaśāyāṃ ca guroḥ pratyantare janaḥ || 30||

bandhanaṃ jāyate ghoraṃ sukhahānirmahadbhayam |
pratyahaṃ vātapīḍā ca śaneḥ pratyantare bhavet || 31||

sarvatra bahudhā lābhaḥ strīsaṅgācca viśeṣataḥ |
paradeśabhavā siddhirbudhapratyantare bhavet || 32||

buddhināśo bhayaṃ vighno dhanahānirmahadbhayam |
sarvatra kalahodvegau ketoḥ pratyantare phalam || 33||

yoginībhyo bhayaṃ bhūyādaśvahāniḥ kubhojanam |
strīnāśaḥ kulajaṃ śokaṃ śukrapratyantare bhavet || 34||

jvararogo mahābhītiḥ putrapautrādipīḍanam |
alpamṛtyuḥ pramādaśca raveḥ pratyantare bhavet || 35||

udvegakalaho cintā mānahānirmahadbhayam |
piturvikalatā dehe vidyoḥ raveḥ pratyantare bhavet || 36||

bhagandarakṛtā pīḍā raktapittaprapīḍanam |
arthahānirmahodvegaḥ kujapratyantare phalam || 37||

hemalābho dhānyavṛddhi kalyāṇaṃ suphalodayaḥ |
gurorantardaśāyāṃ ca bhaved gurvantare phalam || 38||

gobhūmihayalābhaḥ syātsarvatra sukhasādhanam |
saṃgraho hyannapānādeḥ śaneḥ pratyantare bhavet || 39||

vidyālābho vastralābho jñānalābhaḥ samauktikaḥ |
suhṛdāṃ saṅgamaḥ sneho budhapratyantare bhavet || 40||

jalabhītistathā cauryaṃ bandhanaṃ kalaho bhavet |
apamṛtyurbhayaṃ ghoraṃ ketoḥ pratyantare dvija || 41||

nānāvidyārthasamprāptirhemavastravibhūṣaṇam |
labhate kṣemasantoṣaṃ bhṛgoḥ pratyantare janaḥ || 42||

nṛpāllābhastathā mitrātpitṛto mātṛto'pi vā |
sarvatra labhate pūjāṃ raveḥ pratyantare janaḥ || 43||

sarvaduḥkhavimokṣaśca muktalābho hayasya ca |
siddhyanti sarvakāryāṇi vidho pratyantare dvija || 44||

śastrabhītirgade pīḍā vahnimāddyamajīrṇatā |
pīḍā śatrukṛtā bhūrirbhaumapratyantare bhavet || 45||

cāṇḍālena viradhaḥ syādbhayaṃ tebhyo dhanakṣatiḥ |
kaṣṭaṃ jīvāntare jñeyaṃ rāhoḥ pratyantare dhruvam || 46||

dehapīḍā kalerbhītirbhayamantyajalokataḥ |
duḥkhaṃ śanyantare nānā śaneḥ prtyantare bhavet || 47||

buddhināśaḥ kalerbhītirannapānādihānikṛt |
dhanhānirbhayaṃ śatroḥ saneḥ pratyantare budhe || 48||

bandhaḥ śatrorgṛhe jāto varṇahānirbahukṣudhā |
citte cintā bhayaṃ trāsaḥ keto pratyantare bhavet || 49||

cintitaṃ phalitaṃ vastu kalyāṇaṃ svajane sadā |
manuṣyakṛtito lābhaḥ bhṛgiḥ pratyantare dvija || 50||

rājatejo'dhikāritvaṃ svagṛhe jāyate kaliḥ |
jvarādivyādhipīḍā ca raveḥ pratyantare bhavet || 51||

sphītabuddhirmahārambho mandatejā bahuvyayaḥ |
bahustrībhiḥ samaṃ bhogo vidhoḥ pratyantare śanau || 52||

tejohāni putraghāto vahnibhītī riporbhayam |
vātapittakṛtā pīḍā kujapratyantare bhavet || 53||

dhananāśo vastrahānirbhūmināśo bhayaṃ bhavet |
videśagamanaṃ mṛtyuḥ rāho pratyantare śanau || 54||

gṛheṣu svīkṛtaṃ chidraṃ hyasamartho nirīkṣaṇe |
atha vā kalimudvegaṃ guroḥ pratyantare vadet || 55||

buddhirvidyārthalābho vā vastralābho mahatsukham |
budhāsyāntardaśāyāñca budhapratyantare bhavet || 56||

kaṭhinānnasya samprāptirudare rogasambhavaḥ |
kāmalaṃ raktapittaṃ ca ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 57||

uttarasyāṃ bhavellābho hāniḥ syāttu catuṣpadāt |
adhikāro nṛpāgāre bhṛgoḥ prtyanatare bhavet || 58||

tejohānirbhavedrogastanupīḍā yadā kadā |
jāyate cittavaikalyaṃ raveḥ pratyantare budhe || 59||

strīlābhaścārthasampattiḥ kanyālābho mahaddhanam |
labhate sarvataḥ saukhyaṃ vidhoḥ prtyantare janaḥ || 60||

dharmadhīdhanasamprāptiścaurāgnyādiprapīḍanam |
raktavastraṃ śastraghātaṃ bhaumapratyantare bhavet || 61||

kalaho jāyate strībhirakasmādbhayasambhavaḥ |
rājaśastrākṛtā bhītiḥ rāhiḥ prtyantare dvija || 62||

rājyaṃ rājyādhikāro vā pūjā rājasamudbhavā |
vidyābuddhisamṛddhiśca guroḥ pratyantare bhavet || 63||

vātapittamahāpīḍā dehaghātasamudbhavā |
dhananāśamavāpnoti śaneḥ pratyantare janaḥ || 64||

āpatsamudbhavo'kasmāddeśantarasamāgamaḥ |
ketvantare'rthahāniśca ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 65||

mlecchabhīrarthanāśo vā netrarogaḥ śirovyathā |
hāniścatuṣpadānāṃ ca bhṛgoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 66||

mitraiḥ saha virodhaśca svalpamṛtyuḥ parājayaḥ |
matibhraṃśo vivādaśca raveḥ prtyantare bhavet || 67||

annanāśo yaśohānirdehapīḍā matibhramaḥ |
āmavātādivṛddhiścavidhoḥ prtyantare bhavet || 68||

śastraghātena pātena pīḍito vahnipīḍayā |
nīcādbhītī ripoḥ śaṅkā kujapratyantare bhavet || 69||

kāminībhyo bhayaṃ bhūyāttathā vairisamudbhavaḥ |
kṣudrādapi bhavedbhītī rāhoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 70||

dhanahānirmahotpāto sa/stramitravināśanam |
sarvatra labhate kleśaṃ guroḥ pratyantare phalam || 71||

gomahiṣyādimaraṇaṃ dehapīḍā suhṛdvadhaḥ |
svalpālpalābhakaraṇaṃ śaneḥ pratyantare phalam || 72||

buddhināśo mahodvego vidyāhānirmahābhayam |
kāryasiddhirna jāyate jñasya pratyantare phalam || 73||

śvetāśvavastramuktādyaṃ divyastrījaṅgajaṃ sukham |
labhate śukrantare prāpte śukrapratyantare janaḥ || 74||

vātajvaraḥ śiraḥpīḍā rājñaḥ pīḍā riporapi |
jāyate svalpalābho'pi raveḥ pratyantare phalam || 75||

kanyājanma nṛpāllābho vastrābharaṇasaṃyutaḥ |
rājyādhikārasaṃprāptiḥ candrapratyantare bhavet || 76||

raktapittādirogaśca kalahastāḍanaṃ bhavet |
mahānkleśo bhavedata kujapratyantare dvija || 77||

kalaho jāyate strībhirakasmādbhayasambhavaḥ |
rājataḥ śatrutaḥ pīḍā rāhoḥ pratyantare bhavet || 78||

mahaddravyaṃ mahadrājyaṃ vastrmuktādibhūṣaṇam |
gajāśvādipadaprāptiḥ guroḥ pratyantare bhavet || 79||

kharoṣṭrachāgasamprāptirlohamāṣatilādikam |
labhate svalpapīḍādi śaneḥ pratyantare janaḥ || 80||

dhanajñānamahallābho rājarājyādikāritā |
nikṣepāddhanalābho'pi jñasya pratyantare bhavet || 81||

apamṛtyubhayaṃ jñeyaṃ deśāddeśāntarāgamaḥ |
lābho'pi jāyate madhye ketoḥ pratyantare dvija || 82||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

          atha sūkṣmāntardaśādhyāyaḥ || 62||

\medskip

guṇyā svasvadaśāvarṣaiḥ pratyantaradaśāmitiḥ |
khārkraibhaktā pṛthaglabdhiḥ sūkṣmāntaradaśā bhavet || 1||

nijabhūmiparityāgo prāṇanāśabhayaṃ bhavet |
sthānanāśo mahāhāniḥ nijasūkṣmagate  ravau || 2||

devabrāhmaṇbhaktiśca nityakarmaratastathā |
suprītiḥ sarvamitraścaiva raveḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau || 3||

krūrakarmaratistigmaśatrubhiḥ paripīḍanam |
raktasrāvādirogaśca raveḥ sūkṣmagate kuje || 4||

caurāgniviṣabhītiśca raṇe bhaṅgaḥ parājayaḥ |
dānadharmādihīnaśca raveḥ sūkṣmagate hyagau || 5||

nṛpasatkārarājārhaḥ sevakaiḥ paripūjitaḥ |
rājacakṣurgataḥ śāntaḥ sūryasūkṣmagate gurau || 6||

cauryasāhasakarmārthaṃ devabrāhmaṇapīḍanam |
sthānacyutiṃ manodukhaṃ raveḥ sūkṣmagate śanau || 7||

divyāmbarādilabdhiśca divyastrīparibhogitā |
acintitārthasiddhiśca raveḥ sūkṣmagate budhe || 8||

gurutārthavināśaśca bhṛtyadārabhavastathā |
kvacitsevakasambandho raveḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje || 9||

putramitrakalatrādisākhyasampanna eva ca |
nānāvidhā ca sampattī raveḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau || 10||

bhūṣaṇaṃ bhūmilābhaśca sammānaṃ nṛpapūjanam |
tāmasattvaṃ gurutvaṃ ca nijasūkṣmagate vidhau || 11||

duḥkhaṃ śatruvirodhaśca kukṣirogaḥ piturmṛtiḥ |
vātapittakaphodrekaḥ vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate kuje || 12||

krodhanaṃ mitrabandhūnāṃ deśatyāgo dhanakṣayaḥ |
videśānnigaḍaprāptirvidhoḥ sūkṣmagatepyagau || 13||

chatracāmarasaṃyuktaṃ vaibhavaṃ putrasampadaḥ |
sarvatra sukhamāpnoti vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate gurau || 14||

rājopadravabhītiḥ syādvyavahāre dhanakṣayaḥ |
caurarvaṃ viprabhītiśca vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate śanau || 15||

rājamānaṃ vastulābho videśādvāhanādikam |
putrapautrsamṛddhiśca vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate budhe || 16||

ātmano vṛttihananaṃ sasyaśṛṅgavṛṣādibhiḥ |
agnisūryādibhītiḥ syādvidhoḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje || 17||

vivāho bhūmilābhaśca vastrābharaṇavaibhavam |
rājyalābhaśca kīrtiśca vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau || 18||

kleśātkleśaḥ kāryanāśaḥ paśudhānyadhanakṣayaḥ |
gātravaiṣamyabhūmiśca vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate ravau || 19||

bhūmihānirmanaḥkhedo hyapasmārī ca bandhuyuk |
purokṣobhamanastāpo nijasūkṣmagate kuje || 20||

aṅgadoṣo janādbhītiḥ pramadāvaṃśanāśanam |
vahnisarpabhayaṃ ghoraṃ bhaume sūkṣmagate'pyahau || 21||

devapūjāratiścātra mantrābhyutthānatatparaḥ |
loke pūjā pramodaśca bhaume sūkṣmagate gurau || 22||

bandhanānmucyate baddho dhanadhānyaparicchadaḥ |
bhṛtyārthabahulaḥ śrīmān bhaume sūkṣmagate śanau || 23||

vāhanaṃ chātrasaṃyuktaṃ rājyabhogaparaṃ sukham |
kāmaśvāsādikā pīḍā bhaume sūkṣmagate budhe || 24||

parapretitabuddhiśca sarvatrā'pi ca garhitā |
aśuciḥ sarvakāleṣu bhaume sūkṣmagate dhvaje || 25||

iṣṭastrībhogasampattiriṣṭabhojanasaṃgrahaḥ |
iṣṭārthasyāpi lābhaśca bhaume sūkṣmagate bhṛgau || 26||

rājadveṣo dvijātkleśaḥ kāryābhiprayavaṃcakaḥ |
loke'pi nindyatāmeti bhaume sūkṣmagate ravau || 27||

śuddhatvaṃ dhanasamprāptirdevabhāhmaṇvatsalaḥ |
vyādhinā paribhūyet bhaume sūkṣmagate vidhau || 28||

lokopadravabuddhiśca sarvakārye mativibhramaḥ |
śūnyatā cittadoṣaḥ syāt svīye sūkṣmagate'pyagau || 29||

dīrgharogī daridraśca sarveṣāṃ priyadarśanaḥ |
dānadharmarataḥ śasto rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate gurau || 30||

kumārgātkutsitorthaśca duṣṭaśca parasevakaḥ |
asatsaṅgamatirmūḍho rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate śanau || 31||

strīsambhogamatirvāgmī lokasambhāvanāvṛtaḥ |
annamicchaṃstanuglānī rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate budhe || 32||

mādhuryaṃ mānahāniśca bandhanaṃ cāpramākaram |
pāruṣyaṃ jīvahāniśca rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje || 33||

bandhanānmucyate baddhaḥ sthānamānārthasañcayaḥ |
kāraṇād dravyalābhaśca rāhau sūkṣmagate bhṛgau || 34||

vyaktārśo gulmarogaśca krodhahānistathaiva ca |
vāhanādisukhaṃ sarvaṃ rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate ravau || 35||

maṇiratnadhanavāptirvidyopāsanaśīlavān |
devārcanaparo bhaktyā rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau || 36||

nirjite janavidrāvo jane krodhaśca bandhanam |
cauryaśīlaratirnityaṃ rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate kuje || 37||

śokanāśo dhanādhikyamagnihotraṃ śivārcanam |
vāhanaṃ chatrasaṃyuktaṃ svīye sūkṣmagate gurau || 38||

vratabhaṅgo manastāpo videśe vasunāśanam |
virodho bandhuvairgaśca guroḥ sūkṣmagate śanau || 39||

vidyābuddhivivṛddhiśca sasammānaṃ dhanāgamaḥ |
gṛhe sarvavidhaṃ saukhyaṃ guroḥ sūkṣmagate budhe || 40||

jñānaṃ vibhavapāṇḍitye śāstraśrotā śivārcanam |
agnihotraṃ gurorbhaktirguroḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje || 41||

rogānmuktiḥ sukhaṃ bhogo dhanadhānyasamāgamaḥ |
putradārādisaukhyaṃ ca guroḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau || 42||

vātapittaprakopaśca śleṣmodrekastu dāruṇaḥ |
rasavyādikṛtaṃ śūlaṃ guroḥ sūkṣmagate ravau || 43||

chatracāmarasaṃyuktaṃ vaibhavaṃ putrasampadaḥ |
netrakukṣigatā pīḍā guroḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau || 44||

srtījanācca viṣotpattirbandhanaṃ ca rujobhayam |
deśāntaragamo bhrāntirguroḥ sūkṣmagate kuje || 45||

vyādhibhiḥ paribhūtaḥsyāccaurairapahṛtaṃ dhanam |
sarpavṛścikabhītiśca guroḥ sūkṣmagate'pyagau || 46||

dhanahānirmahāvyādhiḥ vātapīḍā kulakṣayaḥ |
bhinnāhārī mahāduḥkhī nijasūkṣmagate śanau || 47||

vāṇijyavṛtterlābhaśca vidyāvibhavameva ca |
strīlābhaśca mahīprāptiḥ śaneḥ sūkṣmagate budhe || 48||

cauropadravakuṣṭhādivṛttikṣayavigumphanam |
sarvāṅgapīḍanaṃ vyādhiḥ śaneḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje || 49||

aiśvaryamāyudhābhyāsaḥ putralābho'bhiṣecanam |
ārogyaṃ dhanakāmau ca śaneḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau || 50||

rājatejovikāratvaṃ svagṛhe jāyate kaliḥ |
kiñcitpīḍā svadehotthā śaneḥ sūkṣmagate ravau || 51||

sphītabuddhirmahārambho mandatejā bahuvyayaḥ |
strīputraiśca samaṃ saukhyaṃ śaneḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau || 52||

tejohānirmahodvego vahnimāndyaṃ bhramaḥ kaliḥ |
vātapittakṛtā pīḍā śaneḥ sūkṣmagate kuje || 53||

pitṛmātṛvināśaśca manoduḥkhaṃ guruvyayam |
sarvatra viphalatvaṃ ca śaneḥ sūkṣmagate'pyahau || 54||

sanmudrābhogasammānaṃ dhanadhānyavivarddhanam |
chatracāmarasamprāptiḥ śaneḥ sūkṣmagate gurau || 55||

saubhāgyaṃ rājasammānaṃ dhanadhānyādisampadaḥ |
sarveṣāṃ priyadarśī ca nijasūkṣmagate budhe || 56||

bālagrahognibhīstāpaḥ strīgadodbhavadoṣabhāk |
kumārgī kutsitāśī ca baudhe sūkṣmagate dhvaje || 57||

vāhanaṃ dhanasampattirjalajānnārthasambhavaḥ |
śubhakīrtirmahābhogo baudhe sūkṣmagate bhṛgau || 58||

tāḍanaṃ nṛpavaiṣamyaṃ buddhiskhalanarogabhāk |
hānirjanāpavādaṃ ca baudhe sūkṣmagate ravau || 59||

subhagaḥ sthirabuddhiśca rājasanmānasampadaḥ |
suhṛdāṃ gurusaṃcāro baudhe sūkṣmagate vidhau || 60||

agnidāho viṣotpattirjaḍatvaṃ ca daridratā |
vibhramaśca mahodvego baudhe sūkṣmagate kuje || 61||

agnisarpanṛpādbhītiḥ kucchrādiriparābhavaḥ |
bhūtāveśabhramādbhrāntirbaudhe sūkṣmagatepyahau || 62||

gṛhopakaraṇaṃ bhavyaṃ dānaṃ bhogādivaibhavam |
rājaprasādasampattirbaudhe sūkṣmagate gurau || 63||

vāṇijyavṛttilābhaśca vidyāvibhavameva ca |
strīlābhaśca mahāvyāptirbaudhe sūkṣmagate śanau || 64||

putradārādijaṃ duḥkhaṃ gātravaiṣamyameva ca |
dāridryād bhikṣuvṛttiśca naije sūkṣmagate dhvaje || 65||

roganāśa'rthalābhaśca guruviprānuvatsalaḥ |
saṅgamaḥ svajanaiḥ sārddhaketoḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau || 66||

yuddhaṃ bhūmivināśaśca vipravāsaḥ svadeśataḥ |
suhṛdvipātirārtiśca ketoḥ sūkṣmagate ravau || 67||

dāsīdāsasamṛddhiśca yuddhe labdhirjayastathā |
lalitā kīrtirutpannā ketoḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau || 68||

āsane bhayamaśvādeścauraduṣṭādipīḍanam |
gulmapīḍā śirorogaḥ ketoḥ sūkṣmagate kuje || 69||

vināśaḥ strīgurūṇāṃ ca duṣṭastrīsaṅgamāllaghuḥ |
vamanaṃ rudhiraṃ pittaṃ ketoḥ sūkṣmagate'pyagau || 70||

riporvirodhaḥ sampattiḥ sahasā rājavaibhavam |
paśukṣetravināśārtiḥ ketoḥ sūkṣmagate gurau || 71||

mṛṣā pīḍā bhavetkṣudramukhotpattiśca laṅghanam |
strīvirodhaḥ satyahāniḥ ketoḥ sūkṣmagate śanau || 72||

nānāvidhajanāptiśca viprayogo'ripīḍanam |
arthasampatsamṛddhiśca ketoḥ sūkṣmagate budhe || 73||

śatruhānirmahatsaukhyaṃ śaṅkarālayanirmitiḥ |
taḍāgakūpanirmāṇaṃ nijasūkṣmagate bhṛgau || 74||

urastāpo bhramaścaiva gatāgataviceṣṭitam |
kvacillābhaḥ kvaciddhānirbhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate ravau || 75||

ārogyaṃ dhanasampāttiḥ kāryalābho gatāgataiḥ |
buddhividyāvivṛddhiḥ syād bhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau || 76||

jaḍatvaṃ ripuvaiṣamyaṃ deśabhraṃśo mahadbhayam |
vyādhiduḥkhasamṛtpattirbhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate kuje || 77||

rājyāgnisarpajā bhītirbandhunāśo guruvyathā |
sthānacyutirmahābhītirbhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate'pyahau || 78||

sarvatra kāryalābhaśca kṣetrārthavibhavonnatiḥ |
vaṇigvṛttermahālabdhirbhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate gurau || 79||

śatrupīḍā mahadduḥkhaṃ catuṣpādavināśanam |
svagotraguruhāniḥ syād bhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate śanau || 80||

bāṇdhavādiṣu sampattirvyavahāro dhanonnatiḥ |
putradārāditaḥ saukhyaṃ bhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate budhe || 81||

agnirogo mahāpīḍā mukhanetraśirovyathā |
sañcitārthātmanaḥ pīḍā bhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje || 82||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

           atha prāṇadaśāphalādhyāyaḥ || 63||

\medskip

pṛthak khagadaśāvarṣairhanyāt sūkṣmadaśāmitim |
khasūryairvibhajellibdharjñeya prāṇadaśāmitiḥ || 1||

pāūṃścalyaṃ viṣajā bādhā caurāgninṛpajaṃ bhayam |
kaṣṭaṃ sūkṣmadaśākāle ravau prāṇadaśāṃ gate || 2||

sukhaṃ bhojanasampattiḥ saṃskāro nṛpavaibhavam |
udārādikṛpābhiśca raveḥ prāṇagate vidhau || 3||

bhūpopadravamanyārthe dravyanāśo mahadbhayam |
mahatyapacayaprāptī raveḥ prāṇagate kuje || 4||

annodbhavā mahāpīḍā viṣotpattirviśeṣataḥ |
arthāgnirājabhiḥ kleśo raveḥ prāṇagate'pyahau || 5||

nānāvidyārthasampattiḥ kāryalābho gatāgataiḥ |
nṛpaviprāśrame sūkṣme raveḥ prāṇagate gurau || 6||

bandhanaṃ prāṇanāśaśca cittodvegastathaiva ca |
bahubādhā mahāhānī raveḥ prāṇagate śanau || 7||

rājānnabhogaḥ satataṃ rājalāñchānatatpadam |
ātmā santarpayedeevaṃ raveḥ prāṇagate budhe || 8||

anyo'nyaṃ kalahaścaiva vasuhāniḥ parājayaḥ |
gurustrībandhuvirgaiśca sūryaprāṇagate dhvaje || 9||

rājapūjā dhanādhikyaṃ strīputrādibhavaṃ sukham |
annapānādibhogādi sūryaprāṇagate bhṛgau || 10||

strīputrādisukhaṃ dravyaṃ labhate nūtanāmbaram |
yogasiddhiṃ samādhiñca nijaprāṇagate vidhau || 11||

kṣayaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ bandhunāśaṃ raktasrāvānmahadbhayam |
bhūtāveśādi jāyate vidhoḥ prāṇagate kuje || 12||

sarpabhītiviśeṣāṇa bhūtopadravān sadā |
dṛṣṭikṣobho matibhraṃśo vidhoḥ prāṇagate'pyahau || 13||

dharmavṛddhiḥ kṣamāprāptirdevabrāhmaṇapūjanam |
saubhāgyaṃ priyadṛṣṭiśca candraprāṇagate gurau || 14||

sahasā dehapatanaṃ śatrūpadravavedanā |
andhatvaṃ ca dhanaprāptiścandraprāṇagate śanau || 15||

cāmaracchatrasamprāptī rājyalābho nṛpāttataḥ |
samatvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu candraprāṇagate budhe || 16||

śastrāgniripujā pīḍā viṣāgniḥ kukṣirogatā |
putradāraviyogaśca candraprāṇagate dhvaje || 17||

putramitrakalatrāptivideśācca dhanāgamaḥ |
sukhasampattirarthaśca candraprāṇagate bhṛgau || 18||

krūratā kopavṛddhiśca prāṇahānirmanovyathā |
deśatyāgo mahābhītiścandraprāṇagate ravau || 19||

kalaho ripubhirbandhaḥ raktapittādirogabhīḥ |
nijasūkṣmadaśāmadhye kuja prāṇagate phalam || 20||

vicyutaḥ sutadāraiśca bandhūpadravapīḍitaḥ |
prāṇatyāgo viṣeṇaiva bhaumaprāṇagate'pyahau || 21||

devārcanaparaḥ sr/īmānmantānuṣṭhānatatparaḥ |
putrapautrasukhāvāptirbhaumaprāṇagate gurau || 22||

agnibādhā bhavenmṛtyurarthanāśaḥ padacyutiḥ |
bandhubhibandhutāvāptirbhaumaprāṇagate śanau || 23||

divyāmbarasamutpattirdivyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ |
divyāṅganāyāḥ samprāptirbhaumaprāṇagate budhe || 24||

patanotpātipīḍā ca netrakṣobho mahadbhayam |
bhujaṅgād dravyahāniśca bhaumaprāṇagate dhvaje || 25||

dhanadhānyādisampattirlokapūjā sukhāgamā |
nānābhogairbhavedbhogī bhaumaprāṇagate bhṛgau || 26||

jvaronmādaḥ kṣayo'rthasya rājavisnehasambhavaḥ |
dīrgharogī daridraḥ syādbhaumaprāṇagate ravau || 27||

bhojanādisukhaprāptirvastrābharaṇajaṃ sukham |
śītoṣṇavyādhipīḍā ca bhaumaprāṇagate vidhau || 28||

annāśane viraktaśca viṣabhītistathaiva ca |
sāhasāddhananāśaśca rāhau prāṇagate bhavet || 29||

aṅgasaukhyaṃ vinirbhītirvāhanādeśca saṅgatā |
nīciḥ kalahasamprāptī rāhoḥ prāṇagate gurau || 30||

gṛhadāhaḥ śarīre ruṅ nīcairapahṛta dhanam |
tathā bandhanasamprāptī rāhoḥ prāṇagate śanau || 31||

gurūpadeśavibhavo gurusatkāravarddhanam |
guṇavāñchīlavāṃścāpi rāhoḥ prāṇagate budhe || 32||

strīputrādivirodhaśca gṛhānniṣkramaṇādapi |
sāhasātkāyahāniśca rāhoḥ prāṇagate dhvaje || 33||

chatravāhanasampattiḥ sarvārthaphalasañcayaḥ |
śivārcanagṛhārambho rāhoḥ prāṇagate bhṛgau || 34||

arśādirogabhītiśca rājyopadravasambhavaḥ |
catuṣpādādihāniśca rāhoḥ prāṇagate ravau || 35||

saumanasyaṃ ca sadbuddhiḥ satkāro gurudarśanam |
pāpādbhītirmanaḥsaukhyaṃ rāhoḥ prāṇagate vidhau || 36||

cāṇḍālāgnivaśādbhītiḥ svapadacyutirāpadaḥ |
malinaḥ śvādivṛttiśca rāhoḥ prāṇagate kuje || 37||

harṣāgamo dhanādhikyamagnihotraṃ śivārcanam |
vāhanaṃ chatrasaṃyuktaṃ nija prāṇagate gurau || 38||

vratahānirviṣādaśca videśe dhananāśanam |
virodho bandhuvargaiśca guroḥ prāṇagate śanau || 39||

vidyābuddhivivṛddhiśca loke pūjā dhanāgamaḥ |
strīputrādisukhaprāptirguroḥ prāṇagate budhe || 40||

jñānaṃ vibhavapāṇḍityaṃ śāstrajñānaṃ śivārcanam |
agnihotraṃ gurorbhaktirguroḥ prāṇagate dhvaje || 41||

rogānmuktiḥ sukhaṃ bhogo dhanadhānyasamāgamaḥ |
putradārādijaṃ saukhyaṃ guroḥ prāṇagate bhṛgau || 42||

vātapittaprakopaṃ ca śleṣmodrekaṃ tu dāruṇam |
rasavyādhikṛtaṃ śūlaṃ guroḥ prāṇagate ravau || 43||

chatracāmarasaṃyuktaṃ vaibhavaṃ putrasampadaḥ |
netrakukṣigatā pīḍā guroḥ prāṇagate vidhau || 44||

strījanācca viṣotpattirbandhanaṃ cātinigrahaḥ |
deśāntaragamo bhrāntirguroḥ prāṇagate kuje || 45||

vyādhibhiḥ paribhūtaḥ syāccaurairapahṛtaṃ dhanam |
sarpavṛścikabhītiśca guroḥ prāṇagate'pyahau || 46||

jvareṇa jvalitā kāntiḥ kuṣṭharogodarādiruk |
jalāgnikṛtamṛtyuḥ syānnijaprāṇagate śanau || 47||

dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ ca māṅgalyaṃ vyavahārābhipūjanam |
devabrāhmaṇabhaktiśca śaneḥ prāṇagate budhe || 48||

mṛtyuvedanaduḥkhaṃ ca bhūtopadravasambhavaḥ |
paradārābhibhūtatvaṃ śaneḥ prāṇagate dhvaje || 49||

putrārthavibhavaiḥ saukhyaṃ kṣitipālāditaḥ sukham |
agnihotraṃ vivāhaśca śaneḥ prāṇagate bhṛgau || 50||

akṣipīḍā śirovyādhiḥ sarpaśatrubhayaṃ bhavet |
arthahānirmahākleśaḥ śaneḥ prāṇagate ravau || 51||

ārogyaṃ putralābhaśca śāntipauṣṭikavardhanam |
devabrāhmaṇabhaktiśca śaneḥ prāṇagate vidhau || 52||

gulmarogaḥ śatrubhītirmṛgayā prānanāśanam |
sarpāgniviṣato bhītiḥ śaneḥ prāṇagate kuje || 53||

deśatyāgo nṛpādbhītirmohanaṃ viṣabhakṣaṇam |
vātapittakṛtā pīḍā śaneḥ prāṇagate'pyahau || 54||

senāpatyaṃ bhūmilābhaḥ saṃgamaḥ svajanaiḥ saha |
gauravaṃ nṛpasammānaṃ śaneḥ prāṇagate gurau || 55||

ārogyaṃ sukhasampattirdharmakarmādisādhanam |
samatvaṃ sarvabhuteṣu nijaprāṇagate budhe || 56||

vahnitaskarato bhītiḥ paramādhirviṣodbhavaḥ |
dehāntakaraṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ budhaprāṇagate dhvaje || 57||

prabhutvaṃ dhanasampattiḥ kīrtirdharmaḥ śivārcanam |
putradārādikaṃ saukhyaṃ budhaprāṇagate bhṛgau || 58||

antardāho jvaronmādau bāndhavānāṃ rati striyāḥ |
prāpyate steeyasampattirbudhaprāṇagate ravau || 59||

strīlābhaścārthasampattiḥ kanyālābho dhanāgamaḥ |
labhate sarvataḥ saukhyaṃ budhaprāṇagate vidhau || 60||

patitaḥ kukṣirogī ca dantanetrādijā vyathā |
arśāṃsi prāṇasandeho budhaprāṇagate kuje || 61||

vastrābharaṇasampattirviyogo vipravairitā |
sannipātodbhavaṃ dukhaṃ budhaprāṇagate'pyahau || 62||

gurutvaṃ dhanasampattirvidyā sadguṇasaṃgrahaḥ |
vyavasāyena sallābho budhaprāṇagate gurau || 63||

cauryeṇa nidhanaprāptirvidhanatvaṃ daridratā |
yācakatvaṃ viśeṣeṇa budhaprāṇagate śanau || 64||

aśvapātena ghātaśca śatrutaḥ kalahāgamaḥ |
nirvicāravadhotpattirnijaprāṇagate dhvaje || 65||

kṣetralābho vairināśo hayalābho manaḥsukham |
paśukṣetradhanāptiśca ketoḥ prāṇagate bhṛgau || 66||

steyāgniripubhītiśca dhanahānirmanovyathā |
prāṇāntakaraṇaṃ kaṣṭaṃ ketoḥ prāṇagate ravau || 67||

devadvijaguroḥ pūjā dīrghayātrā dhanaṃ sukham |
karṇe vā locane rogaḥ ketoḥ prāṇagate vidhau || 68||

pittarogo nasāvṛddhirvibhramaḥ sannipātajaḥ |
svabandhujanavidveṣaḥ ketoḥ prāṇagate kuje || 69||

virodhaḥ strīsutādyaiśca gṛhānniṣkramaṇaṃ bhavet |
svasāhasātkāryahāniḥ ketoḥ prāṇagate'pyahau || 70||

sa/stravraṇairmahārogo hṛtpīḍādisamudbhavaḥ |
sutadāraviyogaśca ketoḥ prāṇagate gurau || 71||

mativibhramatīkṣṇatvaṃ krūrakarmaratiḥ sadā |
vyavasanādbandhanaṃ duḥkhaṃ ketoḥ prāṇagate śanau || 72||

kusumaṃ śayanaṃ bhūṣā lepanaṃ bhojanādikam |
saukhyaṃ sarvāṅgabhogyaṃ ca ketoḥ prāṇagate budhe || 73||

jñānamīśvarabhaktiśca santoṣaśca dhanāgamaḥ |
putrapautrasamṛddhiśca nijaprāṇagate bhṛgau || 74||

lokaprakāśakīrtiśca sutasaukhyavivarjitaḥ |
uṣṇādirogajaṃ dukhaṃ śukraprāṇagate ravau || 75||

devārcane karmaratirmantratoṣaṇatatparaḥ |
dhanasaubhāgyasampattiḥ śukraprāṇagate vidhau || 76||

jvaro masūrikāsphoṭakaṇḍūcipiṭakādikāḥ |
devabrāhmaṇapūjā ca śukraprāṇagate kuje || 77||

nityaṃ śatrukṛtā pīḍā netrakukṣirujādayaḥ |
virodhaḥ suhṛdāṃ pīḍā śukraprāṇagate'pyahau || 78||

āyurārogyamaiśvaryaṃ putrastrīdhanavaibhavam |
chatravāhanasaṃprāptiḥ śukraprāṇagate gurau || 79||

rājopadravajā bhītiḥ sukhahānirmahārujaḥ |
nīcaiḥ saha vivādaśca bhṛgoḥ prāṇagate śanau || 80||

santoṣo rājasammānaṃ nānādigbhūmisampadaḥ |
nityamutsāhavrddhiḥ syācchukraprāṇagate budhe || 81||

jīvitātmayaśohānirdhanadhānyaparikṣayaḥ |
tyāgabhogadhanāni syuḥ śukraprāṇagate dhvaje || 82||

evamṛkṣadaśānāṃ hi sāntarāgāṃ mayā dvija |
phalāni kathitānyatra saṃkṣepādeva te'grataḥ || 83||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

         atha kālacakrāntardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ || 64||

\medskip

jagaddhitāya proktāni purā yāni purāriṇā |
tāni cakrāntardaśāphalāni kathayāmyaham || 1||

meṣāṃśe svāntare bhaume jvaraśca vraṇasambhavaḥ |
budhaśukrendujīveṣu sukhaṃ śatrubhayaṃ ravau || 2||

vṛṣāṃśe svāntare saure kalaho rogasambhavaḥ |
vidyālābhastanau saukhyaṃ gurau tatra gate phalam || 3||

deśatyāgo mṛtirvāpi śastraghāto jvaro'thavā |
vṛṣabhasvāṃśake vipra kuje tatra gate phalam || 4||

vastrābharaṇalābhaśca strīsuyogo mahat sukham |
śukrendusutacandreṣu vṛṣabhasvāṃśake phalam || 5||

nṛpād bhayaṃ pitṛmṛtiḥ svavadādyairbhayaṃ ravau |
mithune svāṃśake śukre dhanavastrasamāgamaḥ || 6||

pitṛmātṛmṛterbhītirjvaraśca vraṇasambhavaḥ |
dūradeśaprayāṇaṃ ca mithune svāṃśake kuje || 7||

buddhividyāvivṛddhiśca mahāvibhavasambhavaḥ |
loke mānaśca prītiśca mithene svāṃśake gurau || 8||

videśagamanaṃ vyādhirmaraṇaṃ dhananāśanam |
bandhunāśo'thavā vipra mithune svāṃśake śanau || 9||

vidyāvastrādilābhaśca dāraputrādijaṃ sukham |
sarvatra mānamāpnoti mithune svāṃśake budhe || 10||

karka svāṃśagate candre putradārasukhaṃ mahat |
aiśvaryaṃ labhate loke mānaṃ prītiṃ tathaiva ca || 11||

śatrubhyaśca paśubhyaśca bhayaṃ rājakulāt tathā |
ādhivyādhibhayaṃ caiva karke svāṃśagate ravau || 12||

putradārasuhṛtsaukhyaṃ dhanavṛddhistathaiva ca |
loke mānaṃ yaśaścaiva karkāṃśe budhaśukrayoḥ || 13||

viṣaśastramṛterbhītiṃ jvararogādisambhavām |
pīḍāṃ caiva samāpnoti karke svāṃśagate kuje || 14||

vibhavasyātilābhaśca śarīre'pi sukhaṃ tathā |
nṛpāt sammānalābhaśca karke svāṃśagate gurau || 15||

vādavyādhibhayaṃ ghoraṃ sarpavṛścikato bhayam |
nānākaṣṭamavāpnoti karke svāṃśagate śanau || 16||

siṃhāṃśe svāṃśage bhaume mukharogabhayaṃ diśet |
pittajvarakṛtāṃ vādhāṃ śastrakṣatamathāpi vā || 17||

dhanavastrādilābhaśca strīputrādisukhaṃ tathā |
budhabhārgavayorvipra siṃhāṃśe svāntarasthayoḥ || 18||

uccāt patanabhītiśca svalpadravyasamāgamaḥ |
videśagamanaṃ caiva siṃhe svāntargate vidhau || 19||

bhayaṃ śatrujanebhyaśca jvarādivyāddhisambhavaḥ |
jñānahānirmṛterbhītiḥ siṃhe svāntargate ravau || 20||

dhanadhānyādilābhaṃ ca prasādaṃ dvijabhūpayoḥ |
vidyāvṛddhimavāpnoti siṃhe svāntargate gurau || 21||

kanyāyāṃ svāṃśage saure kaṣṭaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ |
drayāṇaṃ ca jvaraṃ caiva kṣudbhavaṃ vaiklavaṃ tathā || 22||

nṛpaprasādamaiśvaryaṃ suhṛdbandhusamāgamam |
vidyāvṛddhimavāpnoti kanyāyāṃ svāṃśake gurau || 23||

pittajvarabhavā pīḍā videśe gamanaṃ tathā |
śastraghāto'gnibhītiśca kanyāyāṃ svāntare kuje || 24||

bhṛtyaputrārthalābhaśca nānāsukhasamāgamaḥ |
bandhubhārgavacandreṣu kanyāsvāṃśagateṣu ca || 25||

prayāṇaṃ rogabhītiśca kalaho bandhubhiḥ saha |
śastraghātabhayaṃ caiva kanyāṃśe svāṃśage ravau || 26||

tule svāntargate śukre sadbuddhiśca sukhodayaḥ |
strīputradhananavastrādilābho bhavati niścitaḥ || 27||

pitṛkaṣṭaṃ suhṛdvairaṃ śirorogo jvarodayaḥ |
viṣaśastrāgnibhītiśca tule svāntargate kuje || 28||

dravyaratnādilābhaśca dharmakāryaṃ nṛpādayaḥ |
sarvatra sukhasamprāptistule svāṃśagate gurau || 29||

prayāṇaṃ ca mahāvyādhiḥ kṣetradeḥ kṣatireva ca |
śatruvādhā ca kāryeṣu tule svāṃśagate śanau || 30||

putrajanma dhanaprāptiḥ strīsukhaṃ ca manaḥpriyam |
bhāgyodayaśca vijneyastule svāntargate budhe || 31||

śaśāṅkabudhaśukreṣu vṛścike svāṃśageṣu ca |
nānādhānyadhanaprāptirvyādhivināśo mahat sukham || 32||

śatrukṣobhabhayaṃ vyādhimarthanāśaṃ piturbhayam |
śvāpadād bhayamāpnoti vṛścike svāṃśage ravau || 33||

vātapittabhayaṃ caiva masūrīvraṇamādiśet |
agniśastrādibhītiśca vṛścike svāṃśage kuje || 34||

dhanaṃ dhānyañca ratnaṃ ca devabrāhmaṇapūjanam |
rājaprasādamāpnoti vṛścike svāṃśage gurau || 35||

dhanabandhuvināśaśca jāyate mānasī vyathā |
śatruvādhā mahāvyādhirvṛścike svāṃśage śanau || 36||

atidāhaṃ jvaraṃ chardi mukharogaṃ viśeṣataḥ |
nānākleśamavāpnoti cāpāṃśe svāṃśage kuje || 37||

śriyaṃ vidyāṃ ca saubhāgyaṃ śatrunāśaṃ nṛpāt sukham |
bhārgavenducandrāṇāṃ cāpe svasvāṃśake diśet || 38||

bhāryāvittavināśaṃ ca kalahaṃ ca nṛpād bhayam |
dūrayātrāmavāpnoti cāpāṃśe svāṃśage ravau || 39||

dānadharmatapolābhaṃ rājapūjanamāpnuyāt |
bhāryāvibhavalābhaṃ ca cāpe svāṃśagate gurau || 40||

dvijadevanṛpodbhūtaṃ kopaṃ bandhuvināśanam |
deśatyāgamavāpnoti makarasvāṃśage śanau || 41||

devārcanaṃ tapodhyānaṃ sammānaṃ bhūpateḥ kule |
bhārgavajñendujīvānāṃ mṛgāṃśe'ntardaśāphalam || 42||

śirorogaṃ jvaraṃ caiva karapādakṣataṃ diśet |
raktapittātisārāṃśca mṛgasvāṃśagate kuje || 43||

vināśaṃ pitṛbandhūnāṃ jvararogādikaṃ diśet |
nṛpaśatrubhayaṃ caiva mṛgāṃśasvāṃśage śanau || 44||

nānāvidyārthalābhaśca putrastrīmitrajaṃ sukham |
śarīrārogyamaiśvaryaṃ kumbhe svāṃśagate bhṛgau || 45||

jvarāgnicorajā pīḍā śatruṇāṃ ca mahad bhayam |
manovyathāmavāpnoti ghaṭāṃśasvāntare kuje || 46||

nairujyaṃ ca sukhaṃ caiva sammānaṃ bhūpateḥ dvijāt |
manaḥprasādamāpnoti kumbhāṃśasvāṃśage gurau || 47||

dhātutrayaprakopaṃ ca kalahaṃ deśavibhramam |
kṣayavyādhimavāpnoti kuṃbhāṃśasvāṃśage śanau || 48||

putramitradhanastrīṇāṃ lābhaṃ caiva manaḥpriyam |
saubhāgyavṛddhimāpnoti kumbhāṃśasvāṃśage budhe || 49||

vidyāvṛddhimavāpnoti strīsukhaṃ vyādhināśanam |
suhṛtsaṅgaṃ manaḥprītiṃ mīnāṃśasvāṃśage vidhau || 50||

bandhubhiḥ kalahaṃ caiva caurabhītiṃ manovyathām |
sthānabhraṃśamavāpnoti mīnāṃśasvāṃśage ravau || 51||

raṇe vijayamāpnoti paśubhūmisutāgamam |
dhanavṛddhiśca mīnāṃśe svāṃśayorbudhaśukrayoḥ || 52||

pittarogaṃ vivādañca svajanairapi mānavaḥ |
śatruṇāṃ bhayamāpnoti mīnāṃśasvāṃśage kuje || 53||

dhanavastrakalatrāṇāṃ lābho bhūpasamādaraḥ |
pratiṣṭhā bahudhā loke mīnāṃśasvāṃśage gurau || 54||

dhananāśo manastāpo veśyādīnāṃ ca saṅgamāt |
deśatyāgo bhavedvāpi mīnāṃśasvāṃśage śanau || 55||

evaṃ prājñaiśca vijñeyaṃ kālacakradaśāphalam |
antardaśāphalaṃ caiva vāmarkṣe'pyevameva ca || 56||

idaṃ phalaṃ mayā proktaṃ dharmā'dharmakṛtaṃ purā |
tatsarvaṃ pāṇibhirnityaṃ prāpyate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ || 57||

suhṛdo'ntardaśā bhavyā pāpasyāpi dvijottama |
śubhasyāpi ripoścaivamaśubhā ca prakīrtitā || 58||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

         atha kālacakranavāṃśadaśāphalādhyāyaḥ || 65||

\medskip

meṣe tu raktajā pīḍā vṛṣabhe dhānyavarddhanam |
mithune jñānavṛddhiśca karke dhanapatirbhavet || 1||

siṃhabhe śatrubādhā syāt kanyāyāṃ strījanāt sukham |
tulabhe rājamantritvaṃ vṛścike mṛtyuto bhayam || 2||

arthalābho bhaveccāpe meṣasya navabhāgake |
phalamevaṃ vijānīyaṃ daśākāle dvijottama || 3||

makare pāpakarmāṇi kumbhe vāṇijyato dhanam |
mīne sarvārthasiddhiśca vṛścike vahnito bhayam || 4||

tulabhe rājapūjā ca kanyāyāṃ śatruto bhayam |
karke patnījane kaṣṭaṃ siṃhabhe netrapīḍanam || 5||

mithune viṣato bhītirvṛṣasya navamāṃśake |
vṛṣabhe dhanalābhaḥ sthānmeṣe tu jvarasaṃbhavaḥ || 6||

mīne ca mātulaprītiḥ kumbhe śatrupravardhanam |
makare corato bhītiścāpe vidyāvivardhanam || 7||

meṣe tu śastrasaṃghāto vṛṣe tu kalaho bhavet |
mithune sukhamāpnoti mithunāṃśe phalaṃ tvidam || 8||

karkaṭe sukhamāpnoti siṃhe bhūpālato bhayam |
kanyāyāṃ bandhutaḥ saukhyaṃ tulabhe kīrtimāpnuyāt || 9||

vṛścike ca pituḥ kaṣṭaṃ cāpe jñānadhanāgamaḥ |
makare tvayaśo loke kumbhe vāṇijyataḥ kṣatiḥ || 10||

mīne sukhamāpnoti karkāṃśe phalamīdṛśam |
vṛścike kalahaḥ pīḍā tulabhe sukhasampadaḥ || 11||

kanyāyāṃ dhanadhānyāni karke paśugaṇād bhayam |
siṃhe sukhaṃ ca duḥkhaṃ ca mithune śatruvardhanam || 12||

vṛṣe ca sukhasampattiḥ meṣe kaṣṭamavāpnuyāt |
mīne tu dīrghayātrā syāt siṃhāṃśe phalamīdṛśam || 13||

kumbhabhe dhanalābhaḥ syānmakare'pi dhanāgamaḥ |
cāpe bhrātṛjanāt saukhyaṃ meṣe mātṛsukhaṃ vadet || 14||

vṛṣabhe putrasaukhyaṃ ca mithune śatruto bhayam |
karke dārajanaiḥ prītiḥ siṃhe vyādhivivardhanam || 15||

kanyāyāṃ ca sutotpattiḥ kanyāṃśe phalamīdṛśam |
tulabhe dhanasampattirvṛścike bhrātṛtaḥ sukham || 16||

pitṛvargasukhaṃ cāpe mātṛkaṣṭaṃ mṛge vadet |
kumbhe vāṇijyato lābhaṃ mīne ca sukhasampadam || 17||

vṛścike ca strīyāḥ pīḍā tule ca jalato bhayam |
kanyāyāṃ sukhasampattistulāṃśe phalamīdṛśam || 18||

karkabhe dhanahāniḥ syāt siṃhe bhūpālato bhayam |
mithune bhūmilābhaśca vṛśabhe dhanasampadaḥ || 19||

meṣe tu raktajā pīḍā mīne ca sukhamādiśet |
kumbhe vāṇijyato lābho makare ca dhanakṣitaḥ || 20||

cāpe ca sukhasampattirvṛścikāṃśe phalaṃ tvidam |
meṣe ca dhanalābhaḥ syāt vṛṣe bhūmivivarddhanam || 21||

mithune sarvasiddhiḥ syāt karkabhe sukhasampadaḥ |
siṃhe sarvasukhotpattiḥ kanyāyāṃ kalahāgamaḥ || 22||

tule vāṇjyato lābho vṛścike rogajaṃ bhayam |
cāpe putrasukhaṃ vācyaṃ dhanuraṃśe phalaṃ tvidam || 23||

makare putralābhaḥ syāt kumbhe dhanavivardhanam |
mīne kalyāṇamāpnoti vṛścike paśuto bhayam || 24||

tulabhe tvarthalābhaḥ syāt kanyāyāṃ śatruto bhayam |
karkaṭe śriyamāpnoti siṃhe śatru janād bhayam || 25||

mithune viṣato bhītirmṛgāṃśe phalamīdṛśam |
vṛśabhe dhanasampattirmeṣe netrarujo bhayam || 26||

mīnabhe dīrghayātrā syāt kumbhe dhanavivardhanam |
makare sarvasiddhiḥ syāccāpe jñānavivardhanam || 27||

meṣe saukhyavināśaḥ syāt vṛṣabhe maraṇaṃ bhavet |
mithune sukhasampattiḥ kumbhāṃśe phalamīdṛśam || 28||

karkaṭe dhanavṛddhiḥ syāt siṃhe rājāśrayaṃ vadet |
kanyāyāṃ dhanadhānyāni tule vāṇijyato dhanam || 29||

vṛścike jvarajā pīḍā cāpe jñānasukhodayaḥ |
makare strīvirodhaḥ syāt kumbhe ca jalato bhayam || 30||

mīne tu sarvasaubhāgyaṃ mīnāṃśe phalamīdṛśam |
daśādyaṃśakrameṇaiva jñātvā sarvaphalaṃ vadet || 31||

krūragrahadaśākāle śāntiṃ kuryād vidhānataḥ |
tataḥ śubhamavāpnoti taddaśāyāṃ na saṃśayaḥ || 32||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

           athāṣṭakavargādhyāyaḥ || 66||

\medskip

bhagavan bhavatā'khyātaṃ grahabhāvādijaṃ phalam |
bahunāmṛṣivaryāṇāmācāryāṇāṃ ca sammatam || 1||

saṃkarāt tatphalānāṃ ca grahāṇāṃ gatisaṅkarāt |
itthameveti no sarve jñātvā vaktumalaṃ narāḥ || 2||

kalau pāparatānāṃ ca mandā buddhiryuto nṛṇām |
ato'lpabuddhigamyaṃ yat śāstrametad vadasya me || 3||

tattatkālagrahasthityā mānavānāṃ parisphuṭam |
sukhaduḥkhaparijñānamāyuṣo nirṇayaṃ tathā || 4||

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā brahman kathayāmi tavāgrataḥ |
lokeyātrāparijñānamāyuṣo nirṇayaṃ tathā || 5||

saṃkarasyāvirodhañca śāstrasyāpi prayojanam |
janānāmupakārārthaṃ sāvadhānamanāḥ śṛṇu || 6||

lagnādivyayaparyantaṃ bhāvā saṃjñānurūpataḥ |
phaladāḥ śubhasaṃdṛṣṭā yuktā vā śobhanā matāḥ || 7||

te tūccādibhagaiḥ kheṭairna cāstāribhanīcagaiḥ |
pāpairdṛṣṭayutā bhāvāḥ kalyāṇetaradāyakāḥ || 8||

tairaḥtāribhanīcasthairna ca mitrasvabhoccagaiḥ |
evaṃ samānyataḥ proktaṃ horāśāstrajñasūribhiḥ || 9||

mayaiyat sakalaṃ proktaṃ pūrvācāryānuvartinā |
āyuśca lokayātrāṃ ca śāstrasyāsyate prayojanam || 10||

niścetuṃ tanna saknoti vasiṣṭho vā bṛhaspatiḥ |
kiṃ punarmanujāstatra viśeṣāttu kalau yuge || 11||

sāmānyāṃśo viśeṣāṃśo jyotiḥśāstraṃ dvidhoditam |
proktaḥ sāmānyabhāgastu niścayāṃśastu kathyate || 12||

yathā lagnācca candrācca grahāṇāṃ bhāvajaṃ phalam |
tathā'nyebhyo'pi kheṭebhyo vicintyaṃ daivavidvaraiḥ || 13||

ato ravyādikheṭānāṃ salagnānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak |
aṣṭānāṃ sarvabhāvotthaṃ yathoktamaśubhaṃ śubham || 14||

jñātvā'dau karaṇaṃ sthānaṃ bindurekhopalakṣitam |
kramādaṣṭakavargasya vācyaṃ spaṣṭaphalaṃ yathā || 15||

tatusvāyustririṣpheṣu pañca kāme sukhe'rṇavāḥ |
arau bhāgye trayaḥ putre ṣaṭ karau khe bhave ca bhūḥ || 16||

lagnendujīvaśukrajñāstanau sve maraṇe'pi ca |
ravibhaumārki candrāryā vyaye jñendusitāyakāḥ || 17||

sukhe horenduśukrāśca dharme'rkārkikujā arau |
horājñāryendavaḥ kāme bhave daityendrapūjitaḥ || 18||

sahaje'rkārkiśukrāryabhaumāḥ khe gurubhārgavau |
sute'rkārkīndulagnāraśukrāḥ syuḥ karaṇaṃ raveḥ || 19||

bhāgyasvayośca ṣaḍ veśmamṛtihorāsu pañca ca |
mānaduścikyayorekaḥ sute vedā aristriyoḥ || 20||

trayo vyayeṣṭāvāye ca śūnyaṃ śītakarasya tu |
horārkārārkibhṛgavoṅgajñārkendvārkabhārgavāḥ || 21||

jīvorkārkīndulagnārā horendugurubhāskarāḥ |
sitajñāryāḥ kujatanumandāste sitaśītagū || 22||

horārkārārkivijjīvāḥ śaniḥ khaṃ sakalāḥ kramāt |
vyayaveśmasutastrīṣu ṣaḍ sapta dhanadharmayoḥ || 23||

horāmṛtyuvoḥ śarā vedā vikrame khe trayaḥ kṣate |
dvau bhave śūnyamevaṃ syāt karaṇaṃ bhūmijasya tu || 24||

kujasyārkenduvijjīvasita lagnaśanī ca tu |
sitāragurumandāḥ syurdharmokteṣu kujaṃ vinā || 25||

candrāraguruśukrārkilagnāni kujabhāskarī |
jñendvarkasitalagnāryā eṣu śukraṃ vinā tataḥ || 26||

vinā śaniṃ sapta dharme sitendujñā viyattataḥ |
arkārkijñendulagnārāḥ karaṇaṃ procyate kramāt || 27||

tanusvagṛhakarmāridharmeṣvagnirmṛgau karau |
bhrātṛstriyo rasā lābhe śūnyaṃ putre vyaye śarāḥ || 28||

budhāsyarkenduguravo gurusūryabudhāḥ kramāt |
lagnārkārārkicandrāryā jñārkāryā hi budhasya tu || 29||

jīvārendvārkilagnāni śukramannadharāsutāḥ |
jñendulagnārkaśukrāryā jñārkau jīvendulagnakāḥ || 30||

arkāryaśukraḥ śūnyaṃ ca horendvārārkibhārgavāḥ |
rūpaṃ dhanāyayoḥ khe dvau vyaye sapta kṣate'rṇavāḥ || 31||

mṛtivikramayo pañca guroḥ śeṣeṣu vanhiyaḥ |
lagne śukrendumandāḥ sve āye mandaśca vikrame || 32||

lagnārendujñabhṛgavaḥ suterkāryakujā gṛhe |
śukramandendavo dyūne budhaśukraśanaiścarāḥ || 33||

jīvārārkendavaḥ śatrau sarve mandaṃ vinā vyaye |
karmaṇīnduśanī dharme mandāraguravo mṛgau || 34||

lagnārkisitacandrajñāḥ karaṇaṃ ca guroridam |
sutāyurvikrameṣvakṣi tanusvavyayakheṣviṣuḥ || 35||

aṣṭau striyāmarau ṣaḍ bhūrdharme mitre'kṣi khaṃ bhave |
lagne sve'rkāravijjīvamandāḥ sarve ca kāmabhe || 36||

arkāryau vikramasthāne sute'rkārau śubhe raviḥ |
sukhe'kabudhajīvāḥ syurbhaumajñau mṛtibhe dvaja || 37||

śukrārkendvārkilagnāryāḥ śatrau śūnyaṃ bhave vyaye |
horārkibudhaśukrāryāstanvārajñendvināśca khe || 38||

svastrīdharmeṣu saptāṅgaṃ mṛtihorāgṛheṣu ca |
ājñābhrātṛvyaye vedā rūpaṃ śatrau sute śarāḥ || 39||

āye śūnyaṃ śanerevaṃ karaṇaṃ procyate budhaiḥ |
gṛhe tanau ca lagnārkau svastriyośca raviṃ vinā || 40||

hitvā dharme budhaṃ māne lagnāraravicandrajān |
tato bhrātari jīvārkabudhaśukrāḥ kṣate raviḥ || 41||

vyaye lagnendumandārkāḥ sitārkandujñalagnakāḥ |
sute mṛtau budhārkau ca hitvā'ye khaṃ śanervidaḥ || 42||

uktā'nye sthānadātāra iti sthānaṃ vidurbudhāḥ |
atha sthānagrahān vakṣye sukhabodhāya suriṇām || 43||

svāyastanuṣu mandārasūryā jīvabudhau sute |
vikrame jñendulagnāni lagnārkārkikujā gṛhe || 44||

te ca jñendū khabhe cā'ye sarve śukraṃ vinā vyaye |
lagnaśukrabudhāḥ śatrau te ca jīvasudhākarau || 45||

dyūne'rkārārkiśukrāśca dharmerkārārkividguruḥ |
jñendujīvāḥ kujāryau jñārkendvārārkitanūśanāḥ || 46||

jīvaśukrabudhā bhaumabudhaśukraśanaiścarāḥ |
ravīndvārārkilagnāni ravīndvāryajñabhārgavāḥ || 47||

arkajñajīvāḥ śukrendū te ca tau lagnabhūsutau |
sarve śūnyaṃ kramātproktaṃ sthānaṃ śītakarasya ca || 48||

lagnamandakujā bhaumo horājñendudinādhipāḥ |
mandārau jñaravī jñendujīvārkatanubhārgavāḥ || 49||

mandārau tau sita ścārkiḥ kujārkāryārkilagnakāḥ |
sarve gurusitau sthānaṃ bhaumastaivaṃ vidurbudhāḥ || 50||

lagnamandāraśukrajñā lagnārendusitārkajāḥ |
śukrajñau lagnacandrārkisitārā jñārkabhārgavāḥ || 51||

jīvajñārkendulagnāni bhūmiputraśanaiścarau |
tau ca lagnendu śakrāryā mandārārkajñabhārgavāḥ || 52||

lagnamandāraviccandrāḥ sarve jīvajñabhāskarāḥ |
gurorlagne sukhe jīva lagnārākrabudhā dhane || 53||

candraśukrau ca duścikye mandāryārkāḥ śanirvyaye |
sute śukrendulagnajñamandāścandraṃ vinā tvarau || 54||

lagnārāryā'rkendavo'ste mṛgau jīvārkabhūsutāḥ |
dharme śukrārkalagnendubudhā mandaṃ vinā'yabhe || 55||

māne gurubudhārārkaśukrahorāstathā viduḥ |
lagnaśukrendava ste te jñārkyā rāste jñavarjitāḥ || 56||

sutabhe laghnaśaśijaśaśāṅkāryārkibhārgavāḥ |
jñārau śūnyaṃ sitā'rkendugurulagnaśanaiścarāḥ || 57||

sarve raviṃ vinā śukragurumandāśca mānabhe |
sarve kujenduravayaḥ kramāt bhṛgusutasya ca || 58||

śane ravitanū sūryo lagnendukujasūryajāḥ |
lagnārkau jīvamandārāḥ sarve sūryaṃ vinā kṣate || 59||

arko'rkajñau budho'rkāratanujñāḥ sakalāstataḥ |
kujajñaguruśukrāśca kramāt sthānamidaṃ viduḥ || 60||

tanau turye ca vahniḥ syād duścikye dvau dhane śarāḥ |
buddhimṛtyaṃkariḥpheṣu ṣaṭ kheśakṣatarāśiṣu || 61||

rūpaṃstriyāṃ guruṃ tyaktvā lagnasya karaṇaṃ tvidam |
horāsūryendavo lagne lagnārendvinasūryajāḥ || 62||

gurujñau lagnacandrārā lasūcaṃmaṃbusaurayaḥ |
kṣate śukrastathā caikaḥ kāme sarve guruṃ vinā || 63||

mṛgau bhṛgubudhau tyaktvā dharme gurusitau vinā |
karmaṇyāye tathā śukrovyaye sūryenduvarjitāḥ || 64||

lagnasyedaṃ tu saṃproktaṃ karaṇaṃ dvijapuṅgava |
atha sthānaṃ pravakṣyāmi lagnasya dvijapuṅgava || 65||

ārkijñaśukragurvārāḥ saumyadevejyabhārgavāḥ |
hitvā saumyagurū śeṣāḥ sūjñejyabhṛgusūryajāḥ || 66||

tathā jīvabhṛgū buddhau sarve śukraṃ vinā kṣate |
jīva ekastathā dyūne mṛgau saumyabhṛgū tathā || 67||

dharme gurusitāveva khe bhave śukramantarā |
sūryacandrau tathā riṣphe sthānaṃ lagnasya kīrtitam || 68||

karaṇaṃ binduvat lekhyaṃ sthānaṃ rekhāsvarūpakam |
karaṇaṃ tvaśubhadaṃ proktaṃ sthānaṃ śubhaphalapradam || 69||

daśārekhā likhedūrdhvāstiryag rekhāścaturdaśa |
nageśakoṣṭhasaṃyuktaṃ cakramevaṃ prajāyate || 70||

tiryagaṣṭasu koṣṭheṣu vilagnasahitān khagān |
ādyeṣūrdhvādhareṣvevaṃ bhāvasaṃkhyā likhed budhaḥ || 71||

yathoktaṃ vinyaset tatra karaṇaṃ sthānameva vā |
tataḥ śubhā'śubhaṃ jñātvā jātakasya phalaṃ vadet || 72||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

         atha trikoṇaśodhanādhyāyaḥ || 67||

\medskip

evaṃ salagnakheṭānāṃ vidhāyāṣṭakavargakam |
trikoṇaśodhanaṃ kuryādādau sarvaṃṣu rāśiṣu || 1||

trikoṇaṃ kathyate vipra meṣasiṃhadhanūṃṣyatha |
vṛṣakanyāmṛgasyāśca yugmataulighaṭāstathā || 2||

karkavṛścikamīnāśca trikoṇāḥ syuḥ parasparam |
adho'dhaḥ sarvarāśīnāmaṣṭavargaphalaṃ nyaset || 3||

trikoṇeṣu ca yannyūnaṃ tattulyaṃ triṣu śodhayet |
ekasmin bhavane śūnyaṃ tat trikoṇaṃ na śodhayet || 4||

samatve sarvageheṣu sarvaṃ saṃśodhayed budhaḥ |
paścāt vipaścitā kāryamekādhipatiśodhanam || 5||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

          athaikādhipatyaśodhanādhyāyaḥ || 68||

\medskip

pūrvaṃ trikoṇaṃ saṃśodhya rāśīnāṃ sthāpayet phalam |
pṛthak pṛthak tataḥ kuryādekādhipatiśodhanam || 1||

kṣetradvaye phalani syustadā saṃśodhayed yathā |
kṣīṇena saha cānyasmin śudhayed grahavarjite || 2||

ubhayorgrahasaṃyoge na saṃśodhyaḥ kadācan |
grahayukte phalairhīne grahābhāve phalādhike || 3||

ūnena samamanyasmin śodhayed grahavarjite |
phalādhike grahairyukte cānyasmin sarvamutsṛjet || 4||

ubhayatra grahabhāve samatve sakalaṃ tyajet |
sagrahāgrahayostulye sarvaṃ saṃśodhyamagrahe || 5||

kulīrasiṃhayo rāśyoḥ pṛthak kṣetraṃ pṛthak phalam |
saṃśodhyaikādhipatyaṃ hi tataḥ piṇḍaṃ prasādhayet || 6||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

          atha piṇḍasādhanādhyāyaḥ || 69||

\medskip

evaṃ śodhyāvaśeṣāṅkaṃ rāśimānena varddhayet |
grahayukte ca tadrāśau grahamānena varddhayet || 1||

sarveṣāṃ ca punaryogaḥ piṇḍākhyaḥ kathyate dvija |
gosiṃhau daśabhirguṇyau vasubhiryugmavṛścikau || 2||

saptabhistulameṣau ca mṛgakanye ca pañcabhiḥ |
śeṣāḥ svasaṃkhyayā guṇyā grahamānamathocyate || 3||

jīvāraśukrasaumyānāṃ daśāṣṭanagasāyakāḥ |
pañca śeṣagrahāṇāṃ ca mānaṃ proktamidaṃ kramāt || 4||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

        athā'ṣṭakavargaphalādhyāyaḥ || 70||

\medskip

ātmasvabhāvaśaktiśca pitṛcintā raveḥ phalam |
manobuddhiprasādaśca mātṛcintā mṛgāṅkataḥ || 1||

bhrātṛsattvaṃ guṇaṃ bhūmiṃ bhaumenaiva vicintayet |
vāṇijyakarma vṛttiśca suhṛdaṃ ca budhena tu || 2||

guruṇā dehapuṣṭiñca vidyā putrārthasampadaḥ |
bhṛgorvivāhakarmāṇi bhogasthāna ca vāhanam || 3||

veśyāstrījanasaṃyogaṃ śukreṇa ca nirīkṣayet |
āyuśca jīvanopāyaṃ duḥkhaśoka bhayāni ca || 4||

sarvakṣayaṃ ca maraṇaṃ mandenaiva nirīkṣayet |
tattadbhāvaphalāṅkena guṇayed yogapiṇḍakam || 5||

saptaviṃśaodhṛtaṃ śeṣatulyarkṣe yāti bhānujaḥ |
yadā tadā tasya tasya bhāvasyārti vinirdiśet || 6||

arkāśritarkṣānnavamo rāśiḥ pitṛ gṛhaṃ smṛtam |
tadrāśiphalasaṃkhyābhirvardhayed yogapiṇḍakam || 7||

vibhajet saptaviṃśatyā śeṣarkṣe yāti bhānujaḥ |
yadā tadā pitṛkleśo bhavatīti na saṃśayaḥ || 8||

tattrikoṇagate vāpi pitā pitṛsamo'pi vā |
maraṇaṃ tasya jānīyāt pīḍāṃ vā mahatīṃ vadet || 9||

guṇayed yogapiṇḍaṃ vā tadrāśiphalasaṃkhyayā |
arkoddhṛtāvaśeṣarkṣe yadā gacchati bhānujaḥ || 10||

tattrikoṇarkṣakaṃ vāpi pitṛkaṣṭaṃ tadā vadet |
riṣṭapradadaśāyāṃ tu maraṇaṃ kaṣṭamanyadā || 11||

arkāttu turyage rāhau mande vā bhūminandane |
guruśukrekṣaṇamṛte pitṛhā jāyate naraḥ || 12||

lagnāt candrād gurusthāne yāte sūyrasute'thavā |
pāpairdṛṣṭe yute vāpi pitṛnāśaṃ vaded budhaḥ || 13||

lagnāt sukheśvarāriṣṭadaśākāle pitṛkṣayaḥ |
anukūladaśākāle neti cintyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ || 14||

pitṛjanmāṣṭame jātastadīśe lagnage'pi vā |
karoti pitṛkāryāṇi sa evātra na saṃśayaḥ || 15||

sukhanāthadaśāyāntu sukhaprāpteśca saṃbhavaḥ |
sukheśe lagnalābhasthe candrasthānād viśeṣataḥ |
pitṛgehasamāyukte jātaḥ pitṛvaśānugaḥ || 16||

pitṛjanmatṛtīyarkṣe jātaḥ pitṛdhanāśritaḥ |
pitṛkarmagṛhe jātaḥ pitṛtulyaguṇānvitaḥ || 17||

tadīśe lagnasaṃsthe'pi pitṛśreṣṭho bhavennaraḥ |
evaṃ pūrvaktasāmānyaphalaṃ cātrāpi cintayet || 18||

sūryāṣṭavarge yanchūnyaṃ tanmāse vastare'pi ca |
vivāhavratacūḍādi śubhakarma parityajet || 19||

yatra rekhādhikā tatra māse saṃvacare'pi ca |
aniṣṭe'pi ravau jīve śubhakarma samācaret || 20||

evaṃ candrāṣṭavarge ca yatra śūnyaṃ bhaved bahu |
tatra tatra gate candre śubhaṃ karmaṃ parityajet || 21||

candrāccaturtho mātṛprasādagrāmacintanam |
candrāt sukhaphalaṃ piṇḍaṃ varddhayed bhaiśca sambhajet || 22||

śeṣamṛkṣaṃ śanau yāte mātṛhāniṃ vinirdiśet |
tattrikoṇagate cāpi śanau mātṛrujaṃ vadet || 23||

bhaumāṣṭavarge saṃcintyaṃ bhrātṛvikramadhairyakam |
kujāśritāt tṛtīyarkṣaṃ budhairbhrātṛgṛhaṃ smṛtam || 24||

trikoṇaśodhanaṃ kṛtvā yatra syādadhikaṃ phalam |
bhūmerlābho'tra bhāryāyā bhrātṛṇāṃ sukhamuttamam || 25||

bhaumo balavihīnaścad dīrghāyurbhātṛko bhavet |
phalāani yatra kṣīyante tatra bhaume gate kṣatih || 26||

tṛtīyarkṣaphalenātha piṇḍaṃ sambardhya pūrvavat |
śeṣamṛkṣaṃ śanau yāte bhrātṛkaṣṭaṃ vinirdiśet || 27||

budhātturye kuṭumbaṃ ca mātulaṃ mitrameva ca |
budhe phalādhike rāśau gate teeṣāṃ sukhaṃ diśet || 28||

budhāṣṭavargaṃ saṃśodhya śeṣamṛkṣaṃ gate śanau |
kaṣṭaṃ kuṭumbamitrāṇāṃ mātulānāṃ ca nirdiśet || 29||

jīvāt pañcamato jñānaṃ dharmaṃ putraṃ ca cintayet |
tasmin phalāadhike rāśau santānasya sukhaṃ diśet || 30||

bṛhaspateḥ sutasthāne phalaṃ yatsaṃkhyakaṃ bhavet |
śatrunīcagrahaṃ tyaktvā tāvatī santatirdhruvā || 31||

sutabheśanavāṃśaiśca tulyā vā santatirbhavet |
sutabhāvaphalenaivaṃ piṇḍaṃ saṃguṇya pūrvavat || 32||

putrakaṣṭaṃ vijānīyāt śeṣamṛkṣaṃ gate śanau |
evaṃ dharmaṃ ca vidyāṃ ca kalpayet kālacittamaḥ || 33||

śatrusyākaṣṭavargaṃ ca nikṣipyākāśacāriṣu |
yatra yatra phalāni syurbhūyāṃsi kali tatra tu || 34||

vittaṃ kalatraṃ bhūmiṃ ca tattaddeśād vinirdiśet |
śukrājjāmitrato dāralabdhiścintyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ || 35||

jāmitratattrikoṇastharāśidigdeśasambhavā |
sukheduḥkhe striyāścintye piṇḍaṃ samvardhya pūrvavat || 36||

sanaiścarāśritasthānādaṣṭamaṃ mṛtyubhaṃ smṛtam |
tadeva cāyuṣaḥ sthānaṃ tasmādāyurvicintayet || 37||

lagnātprabhṛti mandāntaṃ phalānyekatra kārayet |
tadyogaphalatulyābde vyādhiṃ vairaṃ samādiśet || 38||

evaṃ mandādilagnāntaṃ phalānyekatra yojayet |
tattulyavarṣe jātasya tasya vyādhibhayaṃ vadet || 39||

dvayoryogasame varṣe kaṣṭaṃ mṛtyusamaṃ diśet |
daśāriṣṭasamāyogo mṛtyureva na saṃśayaḥ || 40||

piṇḍaṃ saṃsthāpya guṇayet śaneraṣṭamagaiḥ phalaiḥ |
saptaviṃśatihṛccheṣatulyamṛkṣaṃ gate śanau || 41||

tattrikoṇarkṣage vāpi jātakasya mṛtiṃ vadet |
arkahṛccheṣarāśau vā tattrikoṇe'pi tad vadet || 42||

śanaiścarāṣṭavargeṣu yatra nāsti phalaṃ gṛhe |
tatra naiva śubhaṃ tasya yadā yāti śanaiścaraḥ || 43||

yatra rāśau śubhādhikyaṃ tatra yāte śanaiścare |
jātakasya dhruvaṃ jñeyaṃ tasmin kāle śubhaṃ phalam || 44||

\medskip\hrule\medskip
\medskip\hrule
#endindian

% for multicolumn

%       \begin{multicols}{5} 
%ṭranlsliteration credits: ajarve@fms30/cca/rockvell/com (āhto Jarve)
\medskip\hrule\medskip

        athā'ṣṭavargāyurdāyādhyāyaḥ || 71||

\medskip

athātrāyuḥ pravakṣye'hamaṣṭavargasamudbhavam |
dinadvayaṃ virekhāyāṃ rekhāyāṃ sārdhavāsaram || 1||

dinamekaṃ dvirekhāyāṃ trirakhāyāṃ dinārdhakam |
vedatulyāsu rekhāsu sārdhasaptadinaṃ smṛtam || 2||

dvivarṣaṃ pañcarekhāsu ṣaḍrekhāsu catuḥsamā |
ṣaḍvarṣaṃ saptarekhāsu vasavo'ṣṭāsu vatsarāḥ || 3||

evaṃ yadāgatāyuḥ syāt sarvakheṭasamudbhavam |
tadardhaṃ sphuṭamāyuḥ syādaṣṭavargabhavaṃ nṛṇām || 4||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

        atha samudāyāṣṭakavargādhyāyaḥ || 72||

\medskip

dvādaśāraṃ likheccakaṃ janmalagnādibhairyutam |
sarvāṣṭakaphalānyatra saṃyojya pratibhaṃ nyaset || 1||

samudāyābhidhāno'yamaṣṭavargaḥ prakathyate |
ataḥ phalāni jātānāṃ vijñeyāni dvijottama || 2||

triṃśādhikaphalā ye syū rāśayaste śubhapradāḥ |
pañcaviṃśāditriṃśāntaphalā madhyaphalā smṛtāḥ || 3||

ataḥ kṣīṇaphalā ye te rāśayaḥ kaṣṭaduḥkhadā |
śubhe śreṣṭhaphalān rāśīn yojayenmatimānnaraḥ || 4||

kaṣṭarāśīn sukāryeṣu varjayed dvijasattama |
śreṣṭharāśigataḥ kheṭaḥ śubho'nyatrā'śubhapradaḥ || 5||

tanvādivyayaparyantaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāvphalāni vai |
adhike śobhanaṃ jñeyaṃ hīne hāniṃ vinirdiśet || 6||

madhye madhyaphalaṃ brūyād tattadbhāvasamudbhavam |
madhyāt phalādhike lābho lābhāt kṣīṇagatovyayaḥ || 7||

lagnaṃ phalādhikaṃ yasya bhogavānarthavān hi saḥ |
viparītena dāridryaṃ bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ || 8||

daśāvadiha bhāvānāṃ kṛtvā khaṃḍatrayaṃ budhaḥ |
paśyet pāpasamārūḍhaṃ khaṃḍe kaṣṭakaraṃ vadet || 9||

saumyairyuktaṃ śubhaṃ brūyānmiśrairmiśraphalaṃ yathā |
kramād bālyādyavasthāsu khaṃḍatrayaphalaṃ vadet || 10||

rekhābhiḥ saptabhiryukte māsemṛtyubhayaṃ nṛṇām |
suvarṇaṃ viṃśatipalaṃ dadyāt dvau tilaparvatau || 11||

rekhābhiraṣṭabhiryukte māse mṛtyubaśo naraḥ |
asatphalavināśāya dadyāt karpūrajāṃ tulām || 12||

rekhābhirmavabhiyukte māse sarpabhayaṃ vadet |
aśvaiścaturbhiḥ saṃyuktaṃ rathaṃ dadyācchubhāptaye || 13||

rekhābhirdaśabhiryukte māse śastrabhayaṃ tathā |
dadyācchubhaphalāvāptyai kavacaṃ vajrasaṃyutam || 14||

abhiśāpabhayaṃ yatra rekhā rudrasamā dvija |
dikpalasvarṇaghaṭitāṃ pradadyāt pratimāṃ vidhoḥ || 15||

yukte dvādaśarekhābhirjale mṛtyubhayaṃ vadet |
saśasyabhūmiḥ viprāya datvā śubhaphalaṃ bhavet || 16||

viśvapramitarekhābhirvyāghrānmṛtyubhayaṃ tathā |
viṣṇorhiraṇyagarbhasya dānaṃ kuryāccubhāptaye || 17||

śatrapramitarekhābhiryukte māse mṛterbhayam |
varāhapratimāṃ dadyāt kanakena vinirmitām || 18||

tithitiśca nṛpād bhītirdadyāt tatra gajaṃ dvija |
riṣṭaṃ ṣoḍaśabhirdadyāt mūrtiṃ kalpatarostathā || 19||

saptendubhirvyādhibhayaṃ dadyāt dhenuṃ guḍaṃ tathā |
kalaho'ṣṭendubhirdadyād ratnagobhūriraṇyakam || 20||

aṅkendubhiḥ pravāsaḥ syācchāntiṃ kuryād vidhānataḥ |
viṃśatyā buddhināśaḥ syād gaṇeśaṃ tatra pūjayet || 21||

rogapīḍaikaviṃśatyā dadyād dhānyasya parvatam |
yamāśvibhirbandhupīḍā dadyādādarśakaṃ dvija || 22||

trayoviṃśatrisaṃyukte māse kleśamavāpnuyāt |
sauvarṇīṃ pratimāṃ dadyādraveḥ saptapalairbudhaḥ || 23||

vedāśvibhirbandhuhīno dadyād gidaśakaṃ nṛpaḥ |
sarvarogavināśārthaṃ japahomādikaṃ caret || 24||

dhīhāniḥ pañcaviṃśatyā pūjyā vāgīśvarī tadā |
ṣaḍviṃśatyā'rthahāniḥ syāt svarṇaṃ dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ || 25||

tathā ca saptaviṃśatyā śrīsuktaṃ tatra saṃjapet |
aṣṭaviṃśatisaṃyukte māse māse hāniśca sarvathā || 26||

sūryahomaśca vidhinā karttavyaḥ śubhakāṃkṣibhiḥ |
ekonatriṃśatā cāpi cintavyākulito bhavet || 27||

ghṛtavastrasuvarṇāni tatra dadyāt vicakṣaṇaḥ |
triṃśatā pūrṇadhānyāptiriti jātakanirṇayaḥ || 28||

triṃśādhikāmī rekhābhirdhanaputrasukhāptayaḥ |
catvāriṃśādhikābhiśca puṇyaśrīrupacīyate || 29||

aṣṭavargeṇa ye śuddhāste śuddhāḥ sarvakarmasu |
ato'ṣṭavargasaṃśuddhiraneṣyā sarvakarmasu || 30||

tāvadgocaramanveṣyaṃ yāvanna prāpyate'ṣṭakam |
aṣṭavarge tu samprāpte gocaraṃ viphalaṃ bhavet || 31||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

         atha raśmiphalādhyāyaḥ || 73||

\medskip

atha raśmīn pravakṣyāmi grahāṇāṃ dvijasattama |
din naveṣviṣusaptāṣṭaśarāḥ svocce karo raveḥ || 1||

nīca khaṃ cāntare proktā raśmayaścānupāttaḥ |
nīconaṃ tu grahaṃ bhārdhādhikaṃ cakrādviśodhayet || 2||

svīyaraśmihataṃ ṣaḍbhirbhajet syū raśmayaḥ svakāḥ |
aparairatra saṃskāraviśeṣaḥ kathito yathā || 3||

svoccabhe te triguṇitāḥ svatrikoṇe dvisaṃguṇāḥ |
svame trighnā dvisaṃbhaktā adhimitragṛhe tathā || 4||

vedaghnā rāmasaṃbhaktā mitrame ṣaḍguṇāstataḥ |
pañcabhaktāstathā śatrugṛhe ced dalitāḥ karāḥ || 5||

adhiśatrugṛhe dvighnāḥ pañcabhaktāḥ same samāḥ |
śaniśukrau vinā tārāgrahā aste gatā yadi || 6||

viraśmayo bhavantyevaṃ jñeyāḥ spaṣṭakarā dvija |
raśmiyogavaśādevaṃ phalaṃ vācyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ || 7||

ekādi pañcaparyantaṃ raśmisaṃkhyā bhavedyadi |
daridrā duḥkhasaṃtaptā api jātāḥ kulottame || 8||

parato daśakaṃ yāvat nirdhanā bhāravāsakāḥ |
strīputragṛhahīnāśca jāyante manujā bhuvi || 9||

akādaśasvalpaputrāḥ svalpavittāśca mānavāḥ |
dvādaśasvalpavittāśca dhūrtā mūrkhāśca nirbalāḥ || 10||

cauryakarmaratā nityaṃ cet trayodaśa raśmayaḥ |
caturdaśasu dharmātmā kuṭumbānāṃ ca poṣakāḥ || 11||

kulocitakriyāsakto dhanavidyāsamanvitaḥ |
raśmibhiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ sarvavidyāguṇānvitaḥ || 12||

svavaṃśamukhyo dhanavānityāha bhagavān vidhiḥ |
parataśca kuleśānā bahubhṛtyā kuṭumbinaḥ || 13||

kīrtimanto janaiḥ pūrṇāḥ sarve ca sukhinaḥ kramāt |
pañcāśajjanapālaścedekaviṃśatiraśmayaḥ || 14||

dānaśīlaḥ kṛpāyukto dvāviṃśatisuraśmiṣu |
sukhayuk saumyaśīlaścet trayoviṃśatiraśmayaḥ || 15||

ātriṃśat parataḥ śrīmān sarvasattvasamanvitaḥ |
rājapriyaśca tejasvī janaiśca bahubhirvṛtaḥ || 16||

ata ūrdhvaṃ tu sāmantaścatvāriṃśat karāvadhi |
janānāṃ śatamārabya sahasrāvadhipoṣakaḥ || 17||

ata ūrdhvantu bhūpālaḥ paṃcāśat kariṇāvadhi |
tata ūrdhvakarairvipra cakravartī nṛpo bhavet || 18||

evaṃ prasūtikālotthanabhogakarasambhavam |
kulakramanusāreṇa jātakasya phalaṃ vadet || 19||

kṣatriyaścakravartī vaiśyo rājā prajāyate |
śūdraśca sadhano vipro yajñakarmakriyārataḥ || 20||

uccābhimukhakheṭasya karāḥ puṣṭaphalapradāḥ |
nīcābhimukhakheṭasya tato nyūnaphalaprdāḥ || 21||

sarveṣāmeva kheṭānāmevaṃ raśmivaśāddvija |
śubhaṃ vā'pyaśubhaṃ cāpi phalaṃ bhavati dehinām || 22||

raśmijñānaṃ vinā samyak na phalaṃ jñātumarhati |
tasmādraśmīn prasādhyaiva phalaṃ vācyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ || 23||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

         atha sudarśanacakraphalādhyāyaḥ || 74||

\medskip

athocyate mayā vipra rahasyaṃ jñānamuttamam |
jagatāmupakārāya yat proktaṃ brahmaṇa svayam || 1||

cakraṃ sudarśanaṃ nāma yadvaśāt prasphuṭaṃ phalam |
nṛṇāṃ tanvādibhāvānāṃ jñātuṃ śaknoti daivavit || 2||

janmato mṛtyuparyantaṃ varṣamāsadinodbhavam |
śubhaṃ vā'pyaśubhaṃ sarvaṃ tacchṛṇuṣvaikamānasaḥ || 3||

ekakendrodbhavaṃ ramyaṃ likhed vṛttatrayaṃ dvija |
dvādaśāraṃ ca tat kuryād bhavedevaṃ sudarśanam || 4||

tatrādyavṛtte lagnādyā bhāvā lekhyāḥ sakhecarāḥ |
tadūrdhvavṛtte candrācca bhavāḥ kheṭasamanvitāḥ || 5||

tadūrdhvavṛtte sūryācca kramāt bhavā grahānvitāḥ |
evamekaikabhāve'tra bhavedbhānāṃ trayaṃ trayam || 6||

atra tu prathamo bhāvo lagnenduravibhiryutaḥ |
taṃ prakalpya tanuṃ tvagre jñeyā bhāvā dhanādayaḥ || 7||

tatra tatra grahasthityā jñeyaṃ tattatphalaṃ budhaiḥ |
tanubhāve śubhaḥ sūryo jñeyo'nyatrāśubhapradaḥ || 8||

pāpo'pi svoccarāśistho na bhavatyaśubhapradaḥ |
evaṃ śubhā'śubhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tattadbhāvaphalaṃ vadet || 9||

yo bhāvaḥ svāmisaumyābhyāṃ yukto dṛṣṭo'yamedhate |
pāpairdṛṣṭo yuto yo vā tasya hāniḥ prajāyate || 10||

jñeyaṃ sagrahabhāvasya grahayogasamaṃ phalam |
agrahasya tu bhāvasya grahadṛṣṭisamaṃ phalam || 11||

śubhaireva śubhaṃ pāpairśubhaṃ miśrakhecaraiḥ |
śubhādhike śubhaṃ jñeyamaśubhaṃ tvaśubhādhike || 12||

evaṃ bhāveṣu kheṭānāṃ yogaṃ dṛṣṭiṃ vilokya ca |
tāratamyena vācyāni phalāni dvijasattama || 13||

yatra naiva grahaḥ kaścinna dṛṣṭi kasyacid bhavet |
tadā tadbhāvajaṃ jñeyaṃ tatsvāmivaśataḥ phalam || 14||

śubho'pi śubhavargeṣu hyadhikeṣvaśubhapradaḥ |
pāpo'pi śubhavargeṣu hyadhikeṣu śubhapradaḥ || 15||

svabhoccasya śubhasyātra vargā jñeyāḥ śubhavāhāḥ |
śatroḥ krūrasya nīcasya ṣaḍvargā aśubhapradāḥ || 16||

evaṃ sarveṣu kheṭeṣu bhaveṣvapi dvijottama |
śubhāśubhatvaṃ sañcinyta tatastatphalamādiśet || 17||

yadā sudarśanādeva phalaṃ siddhyati dehanām |
tadā kiṃ munibhiḥ sarvairlagnādeva phalaṃ smṛtam || 18||

iti ma saṃśayo jātastaṃ chettumarhati |
pṛthagbhagau yadā'rkendū lagnādanyatra saṃsthitau || 19||

tadā sudarśanāccakrāt phalaṃ vācyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ |
ekabhe dvau trayo vā cet tadā lagnāt phalaṃ vadet || 20||

atha vipra pravakṣye'haṃ prativarṣādijaṃ phalam |
asmāt sudarśanādeva daśāntaradaśāvaśāt || 21||

tanvādyairvarṣamāśārdhadvikadhasrān pravartayet |
bhaveśādidvādaśānāṃ daśā varṣeṣu kalpayet || 22||

tadādyantardaśāstadvanmāsādau tadbalaiḥ phalam |
taṃ taṃ bhāvaṃ prakalpyāṅkaṃ tattattanvādijaṃ dvija || 23||

tat tallagnāt kendrakoṇāṣṭame saumyāḥ śubhapradāḥ |
yatra bhāve saiṃhikeyo bhavet tadbhāvahānikṛt || 24||

pāpā vā yatra bahavastattadbhāvavināśanam |
viriṣphāriśubhaiḥ pāpaistriṣaḍāyasthitaiḥ śubham || 25||

evaṃ pratyabdamāsādau bhāvānāṃ phalacintanam |
dvādaśānāṃ daśā'vṛttyā daśāścāyuṣi cintayet || 26||

evaṃ sudarśanāccakrād varṣamāsādijaṃ phalam |
jñātvā tathāṣṭavargotthamubhābhyāṃ phalanirṇayaḥ || 27||

ubhayatra samatve hi sampūrṇaṃ tat phalaṃ vadet |
viṣamatve yadādhikyaṃ tatphalaṃ ca balakramāt || 28||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

      atha paṃcamahāpuruṣalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ || 75||

\medskip

atha vakṣyāmyahaṃ pañcamahāpuruṣalakṣaṇam |
svabhoccagatakendrasthairbalibhiśca kujādibhiḥ || 1||

kramaśo rucako bhadro haṃso mālavya eva ca |
śaśaścaite budhaiḥ sarvairmahāntaḥ puruṣāḥ smṛtāḥ || 2||

dīrghānano mahotsāho svacchakāntirmahābalaḥ |
cārubhrūrnīlakeśaśca suruciśca raṇapriyaḥ || 3||

raktaśyāmo'rihantā ca mantraviccoranāyakaḥ |
krūrobhartā manuṣyāṇāṃ kṣāmā'ṅghrirdvijapūjakaḥ || 4||

vīṇāvajradhanuḥpāśavṛṣacakrāṅkitaḥ kare |
mantrābhicārakuśalī dairdhye caiva śatāṃgulaḥ || 5||

mukhadairghyasamaṃ madhyaṃ tasya vijñaiḥ prakīrtitam |
tulyastulāsahasreṇa rucako dvijapuṅgava || 6||

bhunakti vindhyasahyādripradeśaṃ saptatiṃ samāḥ |
śatreṇa vahninā vāpi sa prayāti surālayam || 7||

śārdūlapratibhah pīnavakṣā gajagatiḥ pumān |
pīnājānubhujaḥ prājñaścaturasraśca yogavit || 8||

sāttvikaḥ śobhanāṃghraśca śobhanaśmaśrusaṃyutaḥ |
kāmī śaṅkhagadācakraśarakuñjaracihnakaiḥ || 9||

dhvajalāṅgalacihnaiśca cihnitāṃghrikarāmbujaḥ |
sunāsaśśāstravid dhīraḥ kṛṣṇākuñcitakeśabhṛt || 10||

svatantraḥ sarvakāryeṣu svajanaprīṇanakṣamaḥ |
aiśvaryaṃ bhujyate cāsya nityaṃ mitrajanaiḥ paraiḥ || 11||

tulayā tulito bhārapramitaḥ strīsutānvitaḥ |
sakṣemo bhūpatiḥ pāti madhyadeśaṃ śataṃ samāḥ || 12||

haṃso haṃsasvaro gauraḥ sumukhonnatanāsikaḥ |
śleṣmalo madhupiṅgākṣo raktavarṇanakhaḥ sudhīḥ || 13||

pīnagaṇḍasthalo vṛttaśirāḥ sucaraṇo nṛpaḥ |
matsyā'ṅkuśadhanuḥśaṃkhakañjakhaṭvāṅgacihnakaiḥ || 14||

cihnatāṃghrikaraḥ strīṣu kāmārto naiti tuṣṭatām |
ṣaṇṇvatyaṃgulo dairghye jalakrīḍārataḥ sukhī || 15||

gaṅgāyamunayormadhyadeśaṃ pāti śataṃ samāḥ |
vanānte nidhanaṃ yāti bhuktvā sarvasukhaṃ bhuvi || 16||

samauṣṭhaḥ kṛśamadhyaśca candrakāntiruciḥ pumān |
sugandho nātiraktāṅgo na hrasvo nātidīrghakaḥ || 17||

samasvaccharado hastināda ājānubāhudhṛk |
mukhaṃ viśvāṃgulaṃ dairghye vistāre ca daśāṅgulam || 18||

mālavyo mālavākhyaṃ ca deśaṃ pāti sasindhukam |
sukhaṃ saptativarṣāntaṃ bhuktvā yāti sulālayam || 19||

tanudvijamukhaḥ śūro nātihrasvaḥ kṛśodaraḥ |
madhye kṣāmaḥ sujaṃghaśca matimān pararandhravit || 20||

śakto vanādridurgeṣu senānīrdanturaḥ śaśaḥ |
caṃcalo dhātuvādī ca strīśakto'nyadhānānvitaḥ || 21||

mālāvīṇāmṛdaṅgā'strarekhāṅkitakarāṃghrikaḥ |
bhūpo'yaṃ vasudhā pāti jīvan khādrisamāḥ sukhī || 22||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

       atha paṃcamahābhūtaphalādhyāyaḥ || 76||

\medskip

atha pañcamahābhūtacchāyājñānaṃ vadāmi te |
jñāyate yena kheṭānāṃ vartamānadaśā budhaiḥ || 1||

śikhibhūkhāmbuvātānāmadhipā maṅgalādayaḥ |
tattadbalāvaśājjñeyaṃ tattadbhūtabhavaṃ phalam || 2||

sabale maṅgale vahnisvabhāvo jāyate naraḥ |
budhe mahīsvabhāvaḥ syādākāśaprakṛtirgurau || 3||

śukre jalasvabhāvaśca mārutaprakṛtiḥ śanau |
miśrairmiśrasvabhāvaśca vijñeyo dvijasattama || 4||

sūrye vahnisvabhāvaśca jalaprakṛtiko vidhau |
svadaśāyāṃ grahāśchāyāṃ vyaṃjayanti svabhūtajām || 5||

kṣudhārtaścapalaḥ śūraḥ kṛśaḥ prājño'tibhakṣaṇaḥ |
tīkṣno gauratanurmānī vahniprakṛtiko naraḥ || 6||

karpūrotpalafandhāḍhyo bhogī sthirasukhī balī |
kṣamāvān siṃhanādaśca mahīprakṛtiko naraḥ || 7||

śabdārthavit sunītijño pragalbho jñānasaṃyutaḥ |
vivṛtāsyo'tidīrghaśca vyomaprakṛtisambhavaḥ || 8||

kāntimān bhāravāhī ca priyavāk pṛthivīpatiḥ |
bahumitrā mṛdurvidvān jalaprakṛtisambhavaḥ || 9||

vāyutattvādhiko dātā krodhī gauro'ṭanapriyaḥ |
bhūpatiśca durādharṣaḥ kṛśāṅgo jāyate janaḥ || 10||

svarṇadīptiḥ śubhā dṛṣṭiḥ sarvakāryārthasiddhitā |
vijayo dhanalābhaśca vahnibhāyāṃ prajāyate || 11||

iṣṭagandhaḥ śarīre syāt susnigdhanakhadantatā |
dharmārthasukhalābhaśca bhūmicchāyā yadā bhavet || 12||

svaccā gaganajā chāyā vākpaṭutvapradā bhavet |
suśabdaśravaṇodbhūtaṃ sukhaṃ tatra prajāyate || 13||

mṛdutā svasthatā dehe jalacchāyā yadā bhavet |
tadā'bhiṣṭarasasvādasukhaṃ bhavati dehinaḥ || 14||

mālinyaṃ mūḍhatā daityaṃ rogaśca pavanodbhavāḥ |
tadā ca śokasantāpau vāyucchāyā yadā bhavet || 15||

evaṃ phalaṃ budhairjñeyaṃ sabaleṣu kujādiṣu |
nirbaleṣu tathā teṣu vaktavyaṃ vyatyayād dvija || 16||

nīcaśatrubhagaiścāpi viparītaṃ phalaṃ vadet |
phalāptirabalaiḥ kheṭaiḥ svapnacintāsu jāyate || 17||

tadduṣṭaphalaśāntyarthamapi cājñātajanmanām |
phalapaktyā daśā jñeyā vartamānā nabhaḥsadām || 18||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

       atha sattvādiguṇaphalādhyāyaḥ || 77||

\medskip

atho guṇavaśenāhaṃ kathayāmi phalaṃ dvija |
sattvagrahodaye jāto bhavetsattvādhikaḥ sudhīḥ || 1||

rajaḥkheṭodaye vijño rajoguṇasamanvitaḥ |
tamaḥkheṭodaye mūrkho bhavejjātastamo'dhikaḥ || 2||

guṇasāmyayuto jāto guṇasāmyakhagodaye |
evaṃ caturvidhā vipra jāyanto jantavo bhuvi || 3||

uttamo madhyamo nīca udāsīna iti kramāt |
teṣāṃ guṇānahaṃ vakṣye nāradāriprabhāṣitān || 4||

śamo damastapaḥ śaucaṃ kṣāntirārjavameva ca |
alobhaḥ satyavāditvaṃ jane sattvādhike guṇāḥ || 5||

śauryaṃ tejo dhṛtirdākṣyaṃ yuddhe cā'pyapalāyanam |
sādhūnāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ ceti guṇā jñeyā rajo'dhike || 6||

lobhaścāsatyavāditvaṃ jāḍyamālasyameva ca |
sevākarmapaṭutvaṃca guṇā ete tamo'dhike || 7||

kṛṣikarmaṇi vāṇijye paṭutvaṃ paśupālane |
satyāsatyaprabhāṣitvaṃ guṇasāmye guṇā ime || 8||

gataiśca lakṣaṇairlakṣya uttamo madhyamo'dhamaḥ |
udāsīnaśca viprenda taṃ tatkarmaṇi yojayet || 9||

dvābhyāmeko'dhiko yaśca tasyādhikyaṃ nigadyate |
anyathā guṇasāmyaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ dvijasattama || 10||

sevyasevakayorevaṃ kanyakāvarayorapi |
guṇaiḥ sadṛśayoreva prītirbhavati niścalā || 11||

udāsīno'dhamasyaivamudāsīnasya madhyamaḥ |
madhyamasyottamo vipra prabhavatyāśrayo mude || 12||

ato'varā varāt kanya sevyataḥ sevako'varaḥ |
guṇaistataḥ sukhotpattiranyathā hānireva hi || 13||

vīryaṃ kṣetraṃ prasūteśca samayaḥ saṅgatistathā |
uttamādiguṇe heturbalavānuttarottaram || 14||

ataḥ prasūtikālasya sadṛśo jātake guṇaḥ |
jāyate taṃ parīkṣyaiva phalaṃ vācyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ || 15||

kālaḥ sṛjati bhūtani pātyatho saṃharatyapi |
iśvaraḥ sarvalokānāmavyayo bhagavān vibhu || 16||

tacchaktiḥ prakṛtiḥ proktā munibhistriguṇātmikā |
tathā vibhakto'vyakto'pi vyakto bhavati dehinām || 17||

caturdhā'vayavāstasya svaguṇaiśca caturvidhaḥ |
jāyante hyuttamo madhye udāsīno'dhamaḥ kramāt || 18||

uttame tūttamo janturmadhye'ṅge ca madhyamaḥ |
udāsīne hyadāsīno jāyate cā'dhame'dhamaḥ || 19||

uttamāṅgaṃ śaristasya madhyamāṅgamuraḥsthalam |
jaṃghādvayaudāsīnamadhamaṃ padamucyate || 20||

evaṃ guṇavaśādeva kālabhedaḥ prajāyate |
jātibhedastu tadbhedājjāyate'tra carācare || 21||

evaṃ bhagavatā sṛṣṭaṃ vibhunā svaguṇaiḥ samam |
caturvidhena kālena jagadetaccaturvidham || 22||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

        atha naṣṭajātakādhyāyaḥ || 78||

\medskip

janmakālavaśādevaṃ phalaṃ proktaṃ tvayā mune |
yajjanmasamayo'jñāto jñeyaṃ tasya phalaṃ katham || 1||

śubhaṃ vā'pyaśubhaṃ vāpi manujasya purākṛtam |
asti kaścidupāyaścet taṃ bhavān vaktumarhati || 2||

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā vipra lokānugrahamānasā |
kathayāmi tava snehāt phalamajñātajanmanām || 3||

varṣāyanartumāsārdhatithinakṣatrabhādiṣu |
yadajñātaṃ ca tanmānaṃ jñāyate praśnalagnataḥ || 4||

praśnāṅgadvādaśāṃśarkṣasthite janma vadet gurau |
ayanaṃ lagnapūrvārdhe saumyaṃ yāmyaṃ parārdhake || 5||

ṛturlagnadṛkāṇarkṣasvāmibhiḥ śaśirādayaḥ |
śaniśukrakujendujñajīvairgrīṣmastu bhānunā || 6||

ayanartuvirodhe tu parivartyāḥ parasparam |
budhacandra surācāryāḥ kujaśukraśanaiścaraiḥ || 7||

māso dṛkāṇapūrvārdherpūrvo'nyastu parārdhake |
anupātāt tithirjñeyā bhāskarāṃśasamā dvija || 8||

tadvaśādiṣṭakālo yo janmakālasamo hi saḥ |
tatra grahāṃśca bhāvāṃśca jñātvā tasya phalaṃ vadet || 9||

gururdvādaśabhrvarṣaiḥ punastadrāśigo bhavet |
tat kasmin paryayo tasya jñeyaḥ saṃvatsaro mune || 10||

saṃvastarasya sandehe praśnakarturdvijottama |
vayo'numānatastatra dvādaśa dvādaśa kṣipet || 11||

tatrāpi saṃśaye jāte gururlagnatrikoṇagaḥ |
kalpyo vayo'numānena vatsaraḥ pūrvavat tataḥ || 12||

jñātvā māsaṃ sasūryāṃśaṃ kālajñānaṃ kathaṃ bhavet |
bhagavanniti me brūhi lokānugrahacetasā || 13||

sakrānteriṣṭasūryāṃśatulye'hni dvijasattama |
raviraudayikaḥ sādhyastasyeṣṭārkasya cāntaram || 14||

kalīkṛtya svaṣaṇnighnaṃ sphuṭārkagatibhājitam |
labdhaṃghaṭyādimānaṃ yat tāvān sūryodayāt param || 15||

pūrvaṃ janmeṣṭakālo hi kramāj jñeyo vipaścitā |
sādhitaudayikādarkādiṣṭe'rke'nikahīnake || 16||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

         atha pravrajyāyogādhyāyaḥ || 79||

\medskip

atha vipra pravakṣyāmi yogaṃ pravrajyakābhidham |
pravrajanti janā yena sampradāyāntaraṃ gṛhāt || 1||

caturādibhirekasthaiḥ pravrajyā balibhiḥ samāḥ |
ravyādibhistapasvī ca kapālī raktavastrabhṛt || 2||

ekadaṇḍī yatiścakradharo nirgranthikaḥ kramāt |
jñeyā vīryādhikasyaiva sabaleṣu bahuṣvapi || 3||

sūryeṇā'staṃ gatāste cedapi vīryasamanvitāḥ |
adīkṣitāstadā jñeyā janāstadgatabhaktayaḥ || 4||

astaṃgatā nirbalāścet sabalaśca raviryadā |
tadā ravibhavā jñeyā pravrajyā dvijasattama || 5||

janmabheśo'nyakheṭaiścedadṛṣṭaḥ śanimīkṣate |
tayorbalavaśāttatra pravrajyāmāpnuyānnaraḥ || 6||

nirbalo janmabheśaścet kevalenārkiṇekṣitaḥ |
tadā śanibhavameva pravrajyāṃ āpnuyājjanaḥ || 7||

śanidṛkkāṇasaṃsthe ca śanibhaumanavāṃśake |
śanidṛṣṭe vidhau jñeyā pravrajyā śanisambhavā || 8||

kujādiṣu jayī śukraḥ saumyago yāmyago'pi vā |
jayī saumyagataścānyaḥ parasparayutau bhavet || 9||

pravrajyākārakaḥ kheṭo yadyanyena parājitaḥ |
tadā labdhāṃ parivrajyāṃ parityajati tāṃ punaḥ || 10||

bahavo janmakāle cet pravrajyākārakā grahāḥ |
balatulyāstadā tatra pravrajyā katamā bhavet || 11||

bahavo balinaścet syuḥ pravrajyākārakā grahāḥ |
tadā prāpnoti sarveṣāṃ teṣāṃ pravrajyakāṃ dhruvam || 12||

tattadgrahadaśākāle pravrajyāṃ yāti tadbhavām |
tyaktvā gṛhītapūrvāṃ tāmanyāṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ || 13||

dṛṣṭeṣvindvijyalagneṣu śaninā navame guruḥ |
rājayoge'tra jāto'sau tīrthikṛnna'tra saṃśayaḥ || 14||

dharmasthānagate mande grahadṛṣṭivivarjite |
rājayoge'tra yo jātaḥ sa rājā dīkṣito bhavet || 15||

\medskip\hrule\medskip

          atha strījātakādhyāyaḥ || 80||

\medskip

bahudhā bhavatā proktaṃ yajjātakaphalaṃ mune |
tannārīṇāṃ kathaṃ jñeyamiti me kathayā'dhunā || 1||

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā vipra tadapi pravadāmyaham |
strīṇāṃ puṃbhiḥ samaṃ jñeyaṃ phalamuktaṃ vipaścitā || 2||

viśeṣastatra yo dṛṣṭaḥ saṃkṣepāt kathayāmi tat |
lagne dehaphalaṃ tasyāḥ pañcame prasavastathā || 3||

saptame patisaubhāgyaṃ vaidhavyaṃ nidhane dvija |
strīṇāmasambhavaṃ yadyat tatphalaṃ tatpatau vadet || 4||

lagnendū samabhe yasyāḥ sā nārī prakṛtisthitā |
kanyocitaguṇopetā suśīlā śubhalakṣaṇā || 5||

śubhekṣitau surūpā ca sadā dehasukhānvitā |
viṣame puruṣākārā duḥśīlā pāpavīkṣitau || 6||

pāpāḍhyau ca guṇairhīnā miśre miśraphalaṃ vadet |
lagnendvoryo balī tasya phalaṃ tasya viśeṣataḥ || 7||

lagnendvoryo balī vipra triṃśāṃśaistadadhiṣṭhitaiḥ |
graharāśivaśād vācyaṃ phalaṃ strīṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ || 8||

kanyaivāragṛhe duṣṭā bhaumatriṃśāṃśake bhavet |
kucaritrā tathā śaukre samāyā bodhane smṛtā || 9||

jaive sādhvī śanau dāsī jñarkṣe kauje chalānvitā |
śaukre prakīrṇakāmā sā baudheṃ'śe ca guṇānvitā || 10||

klībā'rkyaṃśe satī jaive kaujai duṣṭā sitarkṣake |
śaukre khyātaguṇā baudhe kalāsu nipuṇā bhavet || 11||

jaive guṇavatī mānde punarbhūścandrabhe tataḥ |
svatantrā kujātriṃśāṃśe śaukre ca kulapāṃsanā || 12||

baudhe śilpakalā'bhijñā jaive bahuguṇā śanau |
patighnī cārkabhe kauje vācālā bhārgave satī || 13||

baudhe puṃśceṣṭitā jaive rājñī mānde kulacyutā |
kauje bahuguṇā'ryarkṣe śaukre cāpyasatī matā || 14||

baudhe vijñānasaṃyutā jaive'nekaguṇānvitā |
mānde cālparatiḥ proktā dāsī kauje tathā'rkibhe || 15||

suprajñā ca bhavecchaukre baudhe duḥsthā tathā khalā |
jaive pativratā proktā mānde nīcajanānugā || 16||

mande śūnye śubhādṛṣṭe patiḥ kāpuruṣo bhavet |
carabhe ca pravāsī syāt klīvastatra jñamandayoḥ || 17||

sūrye'stabhe patityaktā bālye ca vidhavā kuje |
śanāvaśubhasandṛṣṭe yāti kanyaiva vṛddhatām || 18||

vidhavāstagataiḥ pāpaiḥ saumyaistu sadhavā satī |
miśrakheṭaiḥ pūnarbhūḥ sā jñeyā miśraphalānvitā || 19||

mithoṃ'śasthau sitārau cedanyāsaktā tadā'ṅganā |
saptame ca sthite candre tadā bharturanujñyā || 20||

śukrabhe śanibhe vāpi senduśukre ca lagnage |
mātrā saha tadā nārī vandhakī bhavati dhruvam || 21||

kujarkṣe vā tadaṃśe'ste strīlolaḥ krodhanaḥ patiḥ |
baudharkṣāṃśe tathā vidvān kalāsu nipuṇaḥ sudhīḥ || 22||

jaive sarvaguṇopetaḥ patiraste jitendriyaḥ |
śaukre saubhāgyasaṃyuktaḥ kāntaḥ strījanavallabhaḥ || 23||

saurerkṣa vātha saurāṃśe vṛddho mūrkhaśca saptame |
atīvāmṛdurarkāṃśe tadṛkṣevā'tikarmakṛt || 24||

aste karke tadaṃśe vā kāntaḥ kāmī mṛduḥ patiḥ |
miśre miśraphalaṃ vācyaṃ bhāṃśayośca balakramāt || 25||

sūrye'ṣṭamagate jātā duḥkhadāridryasaṃyutā |
kṣatāṅgī khedayuktā ca bhaveddharmaparāṅmukhī || 26||

candre'ṣṭamagate nārī kubhagā kustano kudṛg |
vastrābharaṇahīnā ca rogiṇī cātigarhitā || 27||

kuje'ṣṭamagate bālā kṛśāṅgī rogasaṃyutā |
vidhavā kāntihīnā ca śokasantāpaduḥkhitā || 28||

budheṣṭamagate jātā dharmahīnā bhayāturā |
abhimānadhanairhīnā nirguṇā kalahapriyā || 29||

gurāvaṣṭamage bālā viśīlā svalpasantatiḥ |
pṛthuvādakarā patyā tyaktā bahvaśanā bhavet || 30||

śukre'ṣṭamagate jātā pramattā dhanavarjitā |
nirdayā dharmahīnā ca malinā kapaṭānvitā || 31||

śanāvaṣṭamage jātā duḥsvabhāvā malimlucā |
pravaṃcanaparā nārī bhavet patisukhojjñitā || 32||

rāhāvaṣṭamabhāvasthe kurūpā pativarjitā |
kaṭhorahṛdayā rogairyuktā ca vyabhicāriṇī || 33||

śaśiśukrau yadā lagne mandarābhyāṃ yutau tadā |
bandhyā bhavati sā nārī sutabhe pāpadṛgyute || 34||

kujāṃśestagate sauridṛṣṭe nārī sarugbhagā |
śubhāṃśe saptame jñeyā subhagā pativallabhā || 35||

budhabhe lagnage sūtau candraśukrayute dvija |
jñeyā pitṛgṛhe nārī sā sarvasukhasaṃyutā || 36||

lagne candrajñaśukreṣu bahusaukhyaguṇānvitā |
jīva tatrātisampannā putravittasukhānvitā || 37||

lagnādaṣṭamagau syātāṃ candrārkau svarkṣagau tadā |
bandhyā'tha kākabandhyā cedevaṃ candrabudhau yadā || 38||

śanimaṅgalabhe lagne candrabhārgavasaṃyute |
pāpadṛṣṭe ca sā nārī bandhyā bhavati niścayāt || 39||

sarāhau saptame sūrye pañcame pāpasaṃyute |
śukrejyarāhavo mṛtyau mṛtāpatyā ca sā bhavet || 40||

śukrejyāvaṣṭame sārau saptame vā kujo bhavet |
śaninā dṛgyuto nārī galadgarbhā prakīrtitā || 41||

pāpakartarike lagne candre jātā ca kanyakā |
samastaṃ pitṛvaṃśaṃ ca pativaṃśaṃ hihanti sā || 42||

sasarpāgnijaleśarkṣe bhānumandāravāsare |
bhadrātithau januryasyāḥ sā viṣākhyā kumārikā || 43||

sapāpaśca śubhau lagne dvau pāpau śatrubhasthitau |
yasyā januṣi sā kanyā viṣākhyā parikīrtitā || 44||

viṣayoge samutpannā mṛtavatsā ca durbhagā |
vastrābharaṇahīnā ca śokasantaptamānasā || 45||

saptameśaḥ śubho vāpi saptame lagnato'thavā |
candrato vā viṣaṃ yogaṃ vinihanti na saṃśayaḥ || 46||

lagne vyaye sukhe vāpi saptame cā'ṣṭame kuje |
śubhadṛgyogahīne ca patiṃ hanti na saṃśayaḥ || 47||

yasmin yoge samutpannā patiṃ hanti kumārikā |
tasmin yoge samutpanno patnīṃ hanti naro'pi ca || 48||

strīhantrā pariṇītā cet patihantrī kumārikā |
tadā vaidhavyayogasya bhaṅgo bhavati niścayāt || 49||

mithoṃ'śasthau mithodṛṣṭau sitārkī vā sitarkṣake |
ghaṭāṃśe lagnage nārī pradīptaṃ madanānalam || 50||

saṃśāntiṃ nayati strībhiḥ sukhībhirmadanāturā |
parābhiḥ puruṣākārasthitabhirdvijasattama || 51||

kujajñaguruśukraiśca balibhiḥ samabhe tanau |
kuśalā'nekaśāstreṣu sā nārī brahmavādinī || 52||

krūre saptamage kaścit khecaro navame yadi |
sā pravrajyāṃ tadāpnoti pāpakhecarasaṃbhavām || 53||

vilagnādaṣṭame saumye pāpadṛgyogavarjite |
mṛtyuḥ prāgeva vijñeyastasya mṛtyurna saṃśayaḥ || 54||

aṣṭame śubhapāpau cet syātāṃ tulyabalau yadā |
saha bhartrā tadā mṛtyuṃ prāptvā svaryāti niścayāt || 55||

\medskip\hrule\medskip
\medskip\hrule
#endindian
\end{document}
